### [32] [SpaAct: Spatially-Activated Transition Learning with Curriculum Adaptation for Vision-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27620)
*Pengna Li,Kangyi Wu,Shaoqing Xu,Fang Li,Hanbing Li,Lin Zhao,Kailin Lyu,Long Chen,Zhi-Xin Yang,Nanning Zheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SpaAct框架，通过两个空间激活任务（动作回顾和未来帧选择）激活视觉语言模型在视觉-语言导航任务中的动态空间感知能力，并引入TriPA渐进式课程学习方法，在VLN-CE基准上达到最优性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 将视觉语言模型（VLM）应用于视觉-语言导航（VLN）时，需要赋予模型两种互补的动态空间感知能力：回溯性动作推理（为什么）和前向转移预测（如何），现有方法对此关注不足。

Method: 提出SpaAct训练框架，包含两个空间激活任务：1) 动作回顾（Action Retrospection），从视觉转换中推断已执行的动作序列；2) 未来帧选择（Future Frame Selection），基于历史信息和动作预测视觉转换。同时设计TriPA三因素渐进式自适应课程学习方法，从易到难组织训练样本。

Result: 在标准VLN-CE基准测试上，SpaAct consistently提升了基于VLM的导航性能，并取得了最优结果（state-of-the-art）。

Conclusion: 通过轻量级的空间激活任务监督和渐进式课程学习，可以有效激活VLM在导航任务中的动态空间感知能力，为VLM在具身导航领域的应用提供了一种有效方案。

Original Abstract: Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) aims to enable an embodied agent to follow natural-language instructions and navigate to a target location in unseen 3D environments. We argue that adapting VLMs to VLN requires endowing them with two complementary capabilities for acquiring such awareness, namely backward action reasoning (why) and forward transition prediction~(how). Based on this insight, we propose SpaAct, a simple yet effective training framework that activates the dynamic spatial awareness in VLMs. Specifically, SpaAct introduces two spatial activation tasks: Action Retrospection, which asks the model to infer the executed action sequence from visual transitions, and Future Frame Selection, which forces the model to predict the visual transitions conditioned on history and action. These two objectives provide lightweight supervision on both backward action reasoning and forward transition prediction, encouraging the model to build dynamic spatial awareness in a VLM-friendly way. To further stabilize adaptation, we design TriPA, a Tri-factor Progressive Adaptive curriculum learning method that organizes training samples from easy to hard, allowing the model to gradually acquire navigation skills from basic locomotion to long-horizon reasoning. Experiments on standard VLN-CE benchmarks show that SpaAct consistently improves VLM-based navigation and achieves state-of-the-art performance. We will release the code and models to support future research.

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言导航（VLN）旨在让具身智能体能够遵循自然语言指令，在未见过的3D环境中导航到目标位置。我们认为，将视觉语言模型（VLM）适配到VLN需要赋予其两种互补的能力来获得这种感知，即回溯性动作推理（为什么）和前向转移预测（如何）。基于这一洞察，我们提出了SpaAct，一个简单而有效的训练框架，用于激活VLM中的动态空间感知能力。具体来说，SpaAct引入了两个空间激活任务：动作回顾（Action Retrospection），要求模型从视觉转换中推断已执行的动作序列；以及未来帧选择（Future Frame Selection），迫使模型根据历史信息和动作预测视觉转换。这两个目标对回溯性动作推理和前向转移预测提供了轻量级监督，以VLM友好的方式鼓励模型构建动态空间感知。为了进一步稳定适配过程，我们设计了TriPA，一种三因素渐进式自适应课程学习方法，将训练样本从易到难组织，使模型能够逐步获得从基本运动到长程推理的导航技能。在标准VLN-CE基准上的实验表明，SpaAct consistently提升了基于VLM的导航性能，并达到了最优水平。我们将开源代码和模型以支持未来研究。

</details>


### [33] [MSR:Hybrid Field Modeling for CT-MRI Rigid-Deformable Registration of the Cervical Spine with an Annotated Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27654)
*Bohai Zhang,Wenjie Chen,Mu Li,Kaixing Long,Xing Shen,Xinqiang Yao,Jincheng Yang,Jianting Chen,Wei Yang,Qianjin Feng,Lei Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对颈椎CT-MRI刚性-可变形混合配准问题，构建了高质量标注的多模态数据集R-D-Reg，并提出了MSR混合配准框架。MSR包含独立椎体刚性配准模块和基于MSL块（Mamba全局建模+Swin Transformer局部建模+自适应门控）的可变形配准模块，通过融合两个变形场生成保持局部解剖一致性的混合场。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 颈椎CT-MRI配准在术前规划中至关重要，但该领域研究不足，尤其缺乏刚性-可变形混合建模方法，同时缺乏高质量标注的多模态数据集限制了研究进展。

Method: 提出MSR框架，包括：(1) 刚性配准模块，对单个椎体进行独立局部刚性对齐；(2) 可变形配准模块，内含MSL块，通过自适应门控融合基于Mamba的全局建模和基于Swin Transformer的局部建模；(3) 融合刚性变形场与可变形变形场生成混合场，保持局部解剖一致性。

Result: 构建并发布了综合标注的CT-MRI数据集R-D-Reg，代码和数据集已在GitHub公开。

Conclusion: MSR框架通过刚性-可变形混合建模有效解决了颈椎复杂关节结构的CT-MRI配准问题，且公开的数据集和代码为后续研究提供了基准。

Original Abstract: Accurate CT-MRI registration of the cervical spine is essential for preoperative planning because this region is anatomically complex,highly variable,and vulnerable to injury of the vertebral arteries and spinal cord. However,cervical CT-MRI registration remains underexplored,particularly for rigid-deformable hybrid modeling,and the lack of high-quality annotated multimodal data further limits progress. To address these challenges, we construct and release a comprehensively annotated CT-MRI dataset, R-D-Reg, and propose MSR, a rigid-deformable hybrid registration framework for complex joint structures. Specifically, MSR includes a rigid registration module for independent local rigid alignment of individual vertebrae and a deformable registration module with an MSL block that combines Mamba-based global modeling and Swin Transformer-based local modeling through adaptive gating. The rigid and deformable deformation fields are then fused to generate a hybrid field that better preserves local anatomical consistency. The code and dataset are publicly available at https://github.com/ssc1230609-spec/MSR-registration.

中文摘要翻译: 精确的颈椎CT-MRI配准对于术前规划至关重要，因为该区域解剖结构复杂、变异性大，且椎动脉和脊髓易受损。然而，颈椎CT-MRI配准仍研究不足，特别是针对刚性-可变形混合建模，同时高质量标注的多模态数据的缺乏进一步限制了进展。为应对这些挑战，我们构建并发布了一个全面标注的CT-MRI数据集R-D-Reg，并提出了MSR——一种针对复杂关节结构的刚性-可变形混合配准框架。具体而言，MSR包括一个用于单个椎体独立局部刚性对齐的刚性配准模块，以及一个带有MSL块的可变形配准模块，该MSL块通过自适应门控将基于Mamba的全局建模与基于Swin Transformer的局部建模相结合。随后，刚性变形场与可变形变形场被融合，生成一个能更好保持局部解剖一致性的混合场。代码和数据集已在https://github.com/ssc1230609-spec/MSR-registration公开。

### [34] [EviMem: Evidence-Gap-Driven Iterative Retrieval for Long-Term Conversational Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27695)
*Yuyang Li,Yime He,Zeyu Zhang,Dong Gong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EviMem提出了一种结合迭代检索与证据差距诊断的闭环框架，通过细粒度记忆层级结构检测检索集缺失信息并驱动查询优化，在长时对话记忆任务中显著提升了时序和多跳问题的回答准确率，同时降低了延迟。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有单次检索无法处理跨会话的时序和多跳问题，而现有迭代方法虽能通过生成内容或文档级信号优化查询，但均未能显式诊断检索集中缺失的证据（即"证据差距"），导致查询优化缺乏针对性。

Method: 提出EviMem框架，包含两个核心组件：1) IRIS（基于不足信号的迭代检索），一个闭环框架，通过充分性评估检测证据差距、诊断缺失内容并驱动有针对性的查询优化；2) LaceMem（对话证据记忆的层次化架构），一种从粗到细的记忆层级结构，支持细粒度的差距诊断。

Result: 在LoCoMo数据集上，相比于MIRIX，EviMem在时序问题上将Judge Accuracy从73.3%提升至81.6%，在多跳问题上从65.9%提升至85.2%，同时延迟降低了4.5倍。

Conclusion: 通过显式诊断并填补检索过程中的证据差距，闭环迭代检索框架能够有效提升长时对话记忆中复杂问题（时序和多跳）的问答性能，同时降低计算开销。

Original Abstract: Long-term conversational memory requires retrieving evidence scattered across multiple sessions, yet single-pass retrieval fails on temporal and multi-hop questions. Existing iterative methods refine queries via generated content or document-level signals, but none explicitly diagnoses the evidence gap, namely what is missing from the accumulated retrieval set, leaving query refinement untargeted. We present EviMem, combining IRIS (Iterative Retrieval via Insufficiency Signals), a closed-loop framework that detects evidence gaps through sufficiency evaluation, diagnoses what is missing, and drives targeted query refinement, with LaceMem (Layered Architecture for Conversational Evidence Memory), a coarse-to-fine memory hierarchy supporting fine-grained gap diagnosis. On LoCoMo, EviMem improves Judge Accuracy over MIRIX on temporal (73.3% to 81.6%) and multi-hop (65.9% to 85.2%) questions at 4.5x lower latency. Code: https://github.com/AIGeeksGroup/EviMem.

中文摘要翻译: 长时对话记忆需要检索分散在多个会话中的证据，但单次检索无法处理时序和多跳问题。现有的迭代方法通过生成内容或文档级信号来优化查询，但都没有显式诊断证据差距（即累积检索集中缺失的内容），导致查询优化缺乏针对性。我们提出了EviMem，它结合了IRIS（基于不足信号的迭代检索）——一个通过充分性评估检测证据差距、诊断缺失内容并驱动有针对性的查询优化的闭环框架，与LaceMem（对话证据记忆的层次化架构）——一种支持细粒度差距诊断的从粗到细的记忆层级结构。在LoCoMo数据集上，EviMem在时序问题（73.3%到81.6%）和多跳问题（65.9%到85.2%）上相比MIRIX提升了Judge Accuracy，同时延迟降低了4.5倍。代码：https://github.com/AIGeeksGroup/EviMem。

### [35] [Deep Learning-Based Segmentation of Peritoneal Cancer Index Regions from CT Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27697)
*Pieter C. Gort,Lotte J. S. Ewals,Marion W. Tops-Welten,Cris H. B. Claessens,Joost Nederend,Fons van der Sommen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出基于深度学习的自动化方法（nnU-Net和Swin UNETR）对CT图像中的放射学腹膜癌指数（rPCI）区域进行分割，nnU-Net取得了接近观察者间一致性的性能（Dice 0.82 vs 0.88），为无创、基于影像的腹膜转移评估奠定了基础。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统腹膜转移评估依赖诊断性腹腔镜计算Sugarbaker腹膜癌指数（sPCI），该过程具有侵入性，且缺乏标准化的影像学评估手段。近期虽定义了放射学PCI（rPCI）的3D区域标准，但尚无自动化的影像分割方法。

Method: 采用nnU-Net和Swin UNETR两个深度学习模型，在62例CT扫描（由三名临床研究者手动标注、两名放射科专家验证的rPCI区域）上进行训练和评估，使用五折交叉验证，评价指标包括Dice相似系数、95% Hausdorff距离和平均表面距离。

Result: nnU-Net整体Dice达到0.82，接近观察者间一致性（0.88），优于Swin UNETR（0.76）；主要挑战集中在右侧腹壁和小肠区域。

Conclusion: 自动化rPCI区域分割是可行的，为无创、基于影像的腹膜转移评估奠定了基础。

Original Abstract: Peritoneal metastases are currently assessed using diagnostic laparoscopy to determine Sugarbaker's Peritoneal Cancer Index (sPCI), which works by dividing the abdomen into 13 regions and scoring each region based on tumor size. A recent consensus study defined 3D regions to facilitate a radiological PCI (rPCI), providing standardized anatomical regions for imaging-based assessment. Despite its clinical value, sPCI is invasive and lacks a standardized imaging counterpart. In this study, we propose a deep learning-based approach to automatically segment the rPCI regions on CT. We evaluate nnU-Net and Swin UNETR on 62 CT scans with rPCI regions manually annotated by three clinical researchers and validated by two expert radiologists. Performance was assessed using five-fold cross-validation with the Dice Similarity Coefficient (Dice), 95th percentile Hausdorff distance and Average Surface Distance. nnU-Net achieved an overall Dice of 0.82, approaching interobserver agreement (0.88) and outperforming Swin UNETR (0.76), with remaining challenges primarily in right flank and small-bowel regions. These results demonstrate feasibility of automated rPCI segmentation, laying the foundation for non-invasive, imaging-based assessment.

中文摘要翻译: 目前，腹膜转移通过诊断性腹腔镜评估Sugarbaker腹膜癌指数（sPCI），该方法将腹腔分为13个区域并根据肿瘤大小对各区域评分。近期一项共识研究定义了3D区域以促进放射学PCI（rPCI）的发展，为基于影像的评估提供了标准化解剖区域。尽管sPCI具有临床价值，但其具有侵入性且缺乏标准化的影像学对应方法。在本研究中，我们提出一种基于深度学习的方法来自动分割CT图像上的rPCI区域。我们在62例CT扫描上评估了nnU-Net和Swin UNETR，这些扫描的rPCI区域由三名临床研究人员手动标注并由两名放射科专家验证。采用五折交叉验证，使用Dice相似系数、95% Hausdorff距离和平均表面距离评估性能。nnU-Net的整体Dice达到0.82，接近观察者间一致性（0.88），优于Swin UNETR（0.76），主要挑战集中在右侧腹壁和小肠区域。这些结果表明自动化rPCI区域分割是可行的，为无创、基于影像的评估奠定了基础。

### [36] [RayFormer: Modeling Inter- and Intra-Ray Similarity for NeRF-Based Video Snapshot Compressive Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27702)
*Yubo Dong,Danhua Liu,Anqi Li,Zhenyuan Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于补丁级光线采样和Inter/Intra-Ray Transformer（RayFormer）的视频快照压缩成像重建方法，通过捕捉内容结构相似性并引入全变分先验，在模拟和真实场景中实现了最先进的 reconstruction 性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于NeRF的视频SCI重建方法采用随机光线采样策略，无法捕捉内容的结构相似性，导致重建质量有限。

Method: 1) 提出补丁级光线采样策略，用于建模内容结构；2) 提出Inter- and Intra-Ray Transformer (RayFormer)，同时捕获同一深度空间邻近点之间的光线间相似性和沿观察光线的相邻点之间的光线内相关性；3) 利用补丁级采样策略，将全变分先验融入目标函数以增强空间平滑性并抑制伪影。

Result: 在模拟场景和真实场景中的实验均表明，所提方法达到了最先进的（SOTA）重建性能。

Conclusion: 通过补丁级采样策略和RayFormer捕捉结构相似性，并引入TV先验，有效提升了视频SCI的重建质量。

Original Abstract: Video snapshot compressive imaging (SCI) enables the reconstruction of dynamic scenes from a single snapshot measurement. Recently, NeRF-based methods have shown promising reconstruction performance. However, such methods typically adopt random ray sampling strategies and fail to capture content structural similarities, resulting in limited reconstruction quality. To address these issues, we first propose a patch-level ray sampling strategy to enable the modeling of content structure. Then, we propose an Inter- and Intra-Ray Transformer (RayFormer) to capture the structural similarities, modeling both inter-ray similarities among spatially neighboring points at the same depth and intra-ray correlations between adjacent points along the viewing ray. Finally, benefiting from the patch-level sampling strategy, the total variation prior is incorporated into the objective function to enhance spatial smoothness and suppress artifacts. Experiments in both simulated and real-world scenes demonstrate that the proposed method achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) reconstruction performance.

中文摘要翻译: 视频快照压缩成像（SCI）能够从单次快照测量中重建动态场景。近年来，基于NeRF的方法展现出了 promising 的重建性能。然而，这类方法通常采用随机光线采样策略，无法捕捉内容的结构相似性，导致重建质量受限。为解决这些问题，我们首先提出了一种补丁级光线采样策略，以实现对内容结构的建模。然后，我们提出了一种光线间与光线内Transformer（RayFormer），用于捕获结构相似性，同时对同一深度空间邻近点之间的光线间相似性和沿观察光线相邻点之间的光线内相关性进行建模。最后，得益于补丁级采样策略，全变分先验被融入目标函数中，以增强空间平滑性并抑制伪影。在模拟场景和真实场景中的实验表明，所提方法达到了最先进的（SOTA）重建性能。

### [37] [A generalised pre-training strategy for deep learning networks in semantic segmentation of remotely sensed images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27704)
*Yuan Fang,Yuanzhi Cai,Jagannath Aryal,Qinfeng Zhu,Hong Huang,Cheng Zhang,Lei Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新颖且简单的预训练策略，通过引导模型在预训练期间避免学习领域特定特征，从而缩小ImageNet与遥感图像之间的域 gap，在四个语义分割数据集上取得了当前最优结果。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 遥感图像分割中，深度学习模型通常使用ImageNet预训练后再微调，但ImageNet与遥感图像之间存在较大的场景和模态域差异，限制了模型性能。虽然建立大规模领域专用预训练数据集可以缓解该问题，但构建成本高、泛化能力有限。因此需要一种不依赖大规模领域数据集、又能提升跨域泛化能力的预训练策略。

Method: 提出一种新型预训练策略，在预训练阶段引导模型避免学习预训练数据集中的领域特定特征，从而增强预训练模型的泛化能力。模型在ImageNet上进行预训练，随后在四个多样化的遥感语义分割数据集上进行微调。

Result: 在四个不同场景和模态的遥感语义分割数据集上均取得最优结果：iSAID 上 67.4% mIoU，MFNet 上 56.9% mIoU，PST900 上 84.22% mIoU，Potsdam 上 91.88% mF1。

Conclusion: 该研究为开发同时适用于计算机视觉和遥感应用的统一基础模型奠定了基础。

Original Abstract: In the segmentation of remotely sensed images, deep learning models are typically pre-trained using large image databases like ImageNet before fine-tuned on domain-specific datasets. However, the performance of these fine-tuned models is often hindered by the large domain gaps (i.e., differences in scenes and modalities) between ImageNet's images and remotely sensed images being processed. Therefore, many researchers have undertaken efforts to establish large-scale domain-specific image datasets for pre-training, aiming to enhance model performance. However, establishing such datasets is often challenging, requiring significant effort, and these datasets often exhibit limited generaliza-bility to other application scenarios. To address these issues, this study introduces a novel yet simple pre-training strategy designed to guide a model away from learning domain-specific features in a pre-training dataset during pre-training, thereby improving the generalisation ability of the pre-trained model. To evaluate the strategy's effectiveness, deep learning models are pre-trained on ImageNet and subsequently fine-tuned on four semantic segmentation datasets with diverse scenes and modalities, including iSAID, MFNet, PST900 and Potsdam. Experimental results show that the proposed pre-training strategy led to state-of-the-art accuracies on all four datasets, namely 67.4% mIoU for iSAID, 56.9% mIoU for MFNet, 84.22% mIoU for PST900, 91.88% mF1 for Potsdam. This research lays the groundwork for developing a unified foundation model applicable to both computer vision and remote sensing applications.

中文摘要翻译: 在遥感图像分割中，深度学习模型通常先使用ImageNet等大型图像数据库进行预训练，然后再针对特定领域数据集进行微调。然而，由于ImageNet图像与所处理的遥感图像之间存在较大的域差距（即场景和模态的差异），这些微调模型的性能常常受到限制。为此，许多研究人员致力于建立大规模领域专用图像数据集用于预训练，以提升模型性能。然而，建立此类数据集往往非常困难，需要投入大量精力，且这些数据集对其他应用场景的泛化能力通常有限。针对这些问题，本研究引入了一种新颖而简单的预训练策略，旨在预训练过程中引导模型避免学习预训练数据集中的领域特定特征，从而提升预训练模型的泛化能力。为评估该策略的有效性，我们在ImageNet上预训练深度学习模型，随后在四个具有不同场景和模态的语义分割数据集上进行微调，包括iSAID、MFNet、PST900和Potsdam。实验结果表明，所提出的预训练策略在所有四个数据集上均达到了当前最优精度：iSAID上mIoU为67.4%，MFNet上mIoU为56.9%，PST900上mIoU为84.22%，Potsdam上mF1为91.88%。本研究为开发同时适用于计算机视觉和遥感应用的统一基础模型奠定了基础。

</details>


### [38] [Linguistically Informed Multimodal Fusion for Vietnamese Scene-Text Image Captioning: Dataset, Graph Framework, and Phonological Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27712)
*Nhi Ngoc-Yen Nguyen,Anh-Duc Nguyen,Nghia Hieu Nguyen,Kiet Van Nguyen,Ngan Luu-Thuy Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对越南语场景文本图像描述任务，提出语音学感知的异构图融合框架PhonoSTFG，并构建了首个大规模越南语场景文本描述数据集ViTextCaps。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有场景文本图像描述方法将文本视为语言无关的模态，不适用于越南语这种声调语言——其变音符号会改变词义、OCR错误普遍、词边界模糊。因此需要将语言特定的结构知识显式融入多模态融合机制中。

Method: 提出HSTFG（异构场景文本融合图），一种带有学习空间注意力偏置的通用图融合框架。通过拓扑分析发现跨模态图边对场景文本融合有害。在此基础上设计PhonoSTFG，专门针对越南语语言推理进行图级融合。

Result: 构建了ViTextCaps数据集（15,729张图像，74,970个标题），语言分析表明52.8%的词汇存在变音符号冲突风险。

Conclusion: 越南语场景文本描述需要语言感知的多模态融合，HSTFG和PhonoSTFG为此提供了有效的图融合框架，ViTextCaps数据集为后续研究提供了基准。

Original Abstract: Scene-text image captioning requires fusing three information streams -- visual features, OCR-detected text, and linguistic knowledge -- to generate descriptions that faithfully integrate text visible in images. Existing fusion approaches treat text as language-agnostic, which fails for Vietnamese: a tonal language where diacritics alter word meaning, OCR errors are pervasive, and word boundaries are ambiguous. We argue that Vietnamese scene-text captioning demands \textit{linguistically informed multimodal fusion}, where language-specific structural knowledge is explicitly incorporated into the fusion mechanism. Motivated from these insights, we propose \textbf{HSTFG} (Heterogeneous Scene-Text Fusion Graph), a general-purpose graph fusion framework with learned spatial attention bias, and show through topology analysis that cross-modal graph edges are harmful for scene-text fusion. Building on this finding, we design \textbf{PhonoSTFG} (Phonological Scene-Text Fusion Graph) which specializes graph-level fusion for Vietnamese linguistic reasoning. To support evaluation, we introduce \textbf{ViTextCaps}, the first large-scale Vietnamese scene-text captioning dataset (\textbf{15{,}729} images with \textbf{74{,}970} captions), with comprehensive linguistic analysis showing that 52.8\% of the vocabulary is at risk of diacritic collision.

中文摘要翻译: 场景文本图像描述需要融合三个信息流——视觉特征、OCR检测到的文本和语言知识——以生成忠实整合图像中可见文本的描述。现有的融合方法将文本视为语言无关的，这对于越南语并不适用：越南语是一种声调语言，变音符号会改变词义，OCR错误普遍存在，词边界模糊不清。我们认为越南语场景文本描述需要\textit{语言感知的多模态融合}，其中语言特定的结构知识被显式地融入融合机制中。基于这些见解，我们提出了\textbf{HSTFG}（异构场景文本融合图），一种带有学习空间注意力偏置的通用图融合框架，并通过拓扑分析表明跨模态图边对场景文本融合有害。基于这一发现，我们设计了\textbf{PhonoSTFG}（语音学场景文本融合图），它将图级融合专门用于越南语语言推理。为支持评估，我们引入了\textbf{ViTextCaps}，首个大规模越南语场景文本描述数据集（\textbf{15,729}张图像，\textbf{74,970}个标题），全面的语言分析表明52.8\%的词汇存在变音符号冲突风险。

### [39] [Improving Calibration in Test-Time Prompt Tuning for Vision-Language Models via Data-Free Flatness-Aware Prompt Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27715)
*Hyeonseo Jang,Jaebyeong Jeon,Joong-Won Hwang,Kibok Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Flatness-aware Prompt Pretraining (FPP)，一种用于测试时提示微调（TPT）的预训练框架，通过在适应前将提示初始化到损失平面的平坦区域，同时提升模型校准质量和分类性能，无需额外标注数据或计算开销。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有TPT方法在提升视觉-语言模型适应性时往往产生校准不良的模型，近期工作通过引入正则化项改善校准但通常牺牲了性能。本文揭示了这些正则化策略隐式促使优化走向平坦极小值，且损失平面的锐度是影响校准质量的关键因素。

Method: 提出Flatness-aware Prompt Pretraining (FPP)，在TPT适应之前对提示进行预训练，将提示初始化到损失平面更平坦的区域。该方法可直接替换现有TPT流程中的初始化部分，无需修改其他组件，不依赖标注数据，也不增加测试时的计算成本。

Result: 仅替换现有TPT流程中的初始化部分，即可同时提升校准质量和分类性能；FPP无需标注数据，测试时调优不产生额外计算开销。

Conclusion: 损失平面的锐度是影响TPT校准质量的关键因素；将提示预训练至平坦区域是一种简单有效且实用的方法，能够在不增加成本的情况下同时改善校准和性能，适合实际部署。

Original Abstract: Test-time prompt tuning (TPT) has emerged as a promising technique for enhancing the adaptability of vision-language models by optimizing textual prompts using unlabeled test data. However, prior studies have observed that TPT often produces poorly calibrated models, raising concerns about the reliability of their predictions. Recent works address this issue by incorporating additional regularization terms that constrain model outputs, which improve calibration but often degrade performance. In this work, we reveal that these regularization strategies implicitly encourage optimization toward flatter minima, and that the sharpness of the loss landscape around adapted prompts is a key factor governing calibration quality. Motivated by this observation, we introduce Flatness-aware Prompt Pretraining (FPP), a simple yet effective pretraining framework for TPT that initializes prompts within flatter regions of the loss landscape prior to adaptation. We show that simply replacing the initialization in existing TPT pipelines--without modifying any other components--is sufficient to improve both calibration and performance. Notably, FPP requires no labeled data and incurs no additional computational costs during test-time tuning, making it highly practical for real-world deployment. The code is available at: https://github.com/YonseiML/fpp.

中文摘要翻译: 测试时提示微调（TPT）通过利用无标签测试数据优化文本提示，已成为增强视觉-语言模型适应性的一项有前景的技术。然而，先前的研究观察到TPT往往产生校准不良的模型，引发对其预测可靠性的担忧。近期工作通过引入额外的正则化项来约束模型输出以解决此问题，这类方法改善了校准但通常降低了性能。在本工作中，我们揭示了这些正则化策略隐式促使优化走向更平坦的极小值，并且适应后提示周围的损失平面锐度是决定校准质量的关键因素。受此观察启发，我们提出了Flatness-aware Prompt Pretraining (FPP)，一个简单而有效的TPT预训练框架，在适应之前将提示初始化到损失平面的平坦区域。我们的实验表明，仅替换现有TPT流程中的初始化部分——而不修改任何其他组件——就足以同时改善校准和性能。值得注意的是，FPP不需要任何标注数据，并且在测试时调优过程中不产生额外的计算开销，使其在实际部署中具有高度的实用性。代码已开源：https://github.com/YonseiML/fpp。

### [40] [Taming Noise-Induced Prototype Degradation for Privacy-Preserving Personalized Federated Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27833)
*Yuhua Wang,Qinnan Zhang,Xiaodong Li,Huan Zhang,Yifan Sun,Wangjie Qiu,Hainan Zhang,Yongxin Tong,Zhiming Zheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VPDR，一种面向原型个性化联邦学习的客户端隐私保护插件，通过方差自适应原型扰动（VPP）和蒸馏引导裁剪正则化（DCR），在保持语义可分性的同时实现更优的隐私-效用权衡。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有原型个性化联邦学习（ProtoPFL）中，各向同性高斯原型扰动（IGPP）方法会对所有维度施加相同噪声，过度扰动具有判别能力的维度，且难以平衡裁剪阈值与表征保真度，导致隐私-效用权衡不佳。

Method: 提出VPDR，包含两个核心模块：(1) 方差自适应原型扰动（VPP），基于维度级类方差反映判别性的观察，对判别性子空间分配更少噪声；(2) 蒸馏引导裁剪正则化（DCR），使特征范数自适应地集中在预定义裁剪阈值附近，同时保持预测一致性。

Result: 理论分析表明，在相同隐私约束下，VPDR的组级机制提供的隐私保证不弱于各向同性基线。在多域基准上的大量实验表明，VPDR在个性化联邦微调中实现了更优的隐私-效用权衡，在鲁棒性方面优于IGPP。

Conclusion: VPDR作为一种客户端侧隐私插件，能无缝集成到现有ProtoPFL框架中，有效缓解各向同性噪声带来的判别性维度过度扰动问题，同时通过自适应裁剪正则化提升表征质量，实现隐私保护与模型性能的双赢。

Original Abstract: Prototype-based Personalized Federated Learning (ProtoPFL) enables efficient multi-domain adaptation by communicating compact class prototypes, but directly sharing them poses privacy risks. A common defense involves per-example $\ell_2$ clipping before prototype computation to bound sensitivity, followed by isotropic Gaussian noise to enforce Local Differential Privacy (LDP). However, Isotropic Gaussian Prototype Perturbation (IGPP) typically over-perturbs discriminative dimensions and struggles to balance the clipping threshold with representation fidelity. In this paper, we propose VPDR, a client-side privacy plug-in that seamlessly integrates into existing ProtoPFLs. Motivated by the observation that dimension-wise class variance reflects discriminability, we introduce Variance-adaptive Prototype Perturbation (VPP), which allocates less noise to discriminative subspaces, preserving semantic separability while ensuring privacy. We further develop Distillation-guided Clipping Regularization (DCR), which enables feature norms to adaptively concentrate near the predefined clipping threshold while maintaining prediction consistency. Theoretical analysis shows that our groupwise mechanism provides privacy guarantees no weaker than the isotropic baseline under the same privacy constraints. Extensive experiments on multi-domain benchmarks demonstrate that VPDR achieves a superior privacy-utility trade-off, outperforming IGPP in personalized federated fine-tuning without sacrificing robustness against realistic attacks.

中文摘要翻译: 基于原型的个性化联邦学习（ProtoPFL）通过通信紧凑的类原型实现高效的多域自适应，但直接共享原型存在隐私风险。一种常见的防御手段是在原型计算前对每个样本进行ℓ2裁剪以限制敏感度，随后添加各向同性高斯噪声以实现局部差分隐私（LDP）。然而，各向同性高斯原型扰动（IGPP）通常会过度扰动具有判别能力的维度，并且在裁剪阈值与表征保真度之间难以取得平衡。本文提出VPDR，一种客户端侧隐私保护插件，可无缝集成到现有ProtoPFL框架中。受维度级类方差反映判别性这一观察的启发，我们引入了方差自适应原型扰动（VPP），对判别性子空间分配更少的噪声，从而在保证隐私的同时保留语义可分性。我们进一步提出了蒸馏引导裁剪正则化（DCR），使特征范数自适应地集中在预定义裁剪阈值附近，同时保持预测一致性。理论分析表明，在相同隐私约束下，我们的组级机制提供的隐私保证不弱于各向同性基线。在多域基准上的大量实验表明，VPDR在个性化联邦微调中实现了更优的隐私-效用权衡，在不牺牲对现实攻击鲁棒性的前提下优于IGPP。

</details>


### [41] [HiMix: Hierarchical Artifact-aware Mixup for Generalized Synthetic Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27903)
*Shuchang Zhou,Kaiwen Shen,Jiwei Wei,Yuyang Zhou,Peng Wang,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对生成模型快速发展导致合成图像检测泛化性差的问题，提出HiMix统一框架，通过混合增强分布和层次化伪造表征学习，在多个基准上实现最先进的泛化性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有合成图像检测器通常在有限且有偏的数据集上训练，导致对未见过的生成器泛化能力差。

Method: 提出HiMix框架，包含两个核心模块：(1) Mixup驱动的分布增强(MDA)模块，通过构建真实与伪造图像之间的连续过渡样本来扩展训练分布；(2) 层次化伪造感知表征(HAR)模块，通过跨层集成和粗到细特征融合，从全局和局部两个层次聚合伪造信息。

Result: 在多个基准上的大量实验表明，HiMix取得了最先进的性能，建立了良好分离的逻辑值，从而提升了对未见伪造图像的泛化能力。

Conclusion: HiMix通过分布增强和层次化伪造感知表征学习有效提升了合成图像检测的泛化性能，在多个基准上达到最优。

Original Abstract: The rapid evolution of generative models has enabled the creation of highly realistic and diverse synthetic images, posing significant challenges to reliable and generalizable Synthetic Image Detection (SID). However, existing detectors are typically trained on limited and biased datasets, resulting in poor generalization to unseen generators. To address this issue, we propose HiMix, a unified framework that enhances generalization by expanding the training distribution and promoting artifact-aware representations. Specifically, the Mixup-driven Distributional Augmentation (MDA) module constructs continuous transitional samples between real and fake images, improving coverage of low-confidence regions and exposing the model to more challenging samples, while the pixel-wise mixup operation smoothly perturbs semantics to enhance sensitivity to low-level artifacts. Moreover, the Hierarchical Artifact-aware Representation (HAR) module aggregates artifact information from both global and local levels through cross-layer integration and coarse-to-fine feature fusion, enabling the extraction of discriminative forgery representations under diverse distributions. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that HiMix achieves state-of-the-art performance, establishing well-separated logits for improved generalization to unseen forgeries.

中文摘要翻译: 生成模型的快速发展使得创建高度逼真且多样化的合成图像成为可能，这对可靠且可泛化的合成图像检测(Synthetic Image Detection, SID)提出了重大挑战。然而，现有检测器通常在有限且有偏的数据集上训练，导致对未见过的生成器泛化能力差。为解决这一问题，我们提出HiMix，一个通过扩展训练分布和促进伪造感知表征来增强泛化能力的统一框架。具体而言，Mixup驱动的分布增强(MDA)模块构建了真实图像与伪造图像之间的连续过渡样本，改善了低置信度区域的覆盖范围并使模型暴露于更具挑战性的样本，而逐像素的mixup操作平滑地扰动语义以增强对低级伪影的敏感性。此外，层次化伪造感知表征(HAR)模块通过跨层集成和粗到细特征融合，从全局和局部两个层次聚合伪造信息，从而能够在多样化分布下提取具有判别力的伪造表征。在多个基准上的大量实验表明，HiMix取得了最先进的性能，建立了良好分离的逻辑值，从而提升了对未见伪造图像的泛化能力。

### [42] [Generate Your Talking Avatar from Video Reference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27918)
*Zujin Guo,Zhenhui Ye,Yi Ren,Yuanming Li,Ce Chen,Zhibin Hong,Chen Change Loy*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TAVR提出了一种基于视频参考的跨场景说话头像生成框架，通过令牌选择模块和三阶段训练（同场景预训练、跨场景微调、身份强化学习），在自定义背景中生成高保真说话视频，显著优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有说话头像方法依赖同场景单张静态参考图像，缺乏充分的时间和表情线索，难以在自定义背景中合成高保真度的说话头像。

Method: TAVR框架包含三个核心组件：(1) 令牌选择模块，用于处理扩展的时间上下文并弥合跨场景领域差异；(2) 三阶段训练方案：同场景视频预训练建立基础外观复制能力，跨场景参考微调实现鲁棒的跨场景适应，任务特定强化学习通过身份奖励最大化身份相似度。

Result: 构建了包含158个精心筛选的跨场景视频对的基准测试，实验表明TAVR受益于灵活的推理时视频参考，在定量和定性上均一致超越现有基线，并已部署到生产环境。

Conclusion: TAVR通过引入跨场景视频输入和系统的三阶段训练范式，有效解决了说话头像生成中跨场景适应和身份保持的关键挑战，为实际生产部署提供了可行方案。

To this end, we introduce Talking Avatar generation from Video Reference (TAVR), a novel framework that shifts the paradigm by leveraging cross-scene video inputs. To effectively process these extended temporal contexts and bridge cross-scene domain gaps, TAVR integrates a token selection module alongside a comprehensive three-stage training scheme. Specifically, same-scene video pretraining establishes foundational appearance copying, which is subsequently expanded by cross-scene reference fine-tuning for robust cross-scene adaptation. Finally, task-specific reinforcement learning aligns the generated outputs with identity-based rewards to maximize identity similarity. Extensive experiments show that TAVR benefits from flexible inference-time video referencing and consistently surpasses existing baselines both quantitatively and qualitatively. This work has been deployed to production. 中文摘要翻译: 现有说话头像方法通常采用基于同场景静态参考图像的图像到视频生成流程。这种受限的单视角方式缺乏充分的时间和表情线索，限制了在自定义背景下合成高保真说话头像的能力。为此，我们提出了基于视频参考的说话头像生成（TAVR），一种通过利用跨场景视频输入来转变现有范式的新型框架。为了有效处理这些扩展的时间上下文并弥合跨场景领域差异，TAVR集成了一个令牌选择模块以及一个全面的三阶段训练方案。具体而言，同场景视频预训练建立了基础的外观复制能力，随后通过跨场景参考微调实现鲁棒的跨场景适应。最后，任务特定的强化学习将生成输出与基于身份奖励的对齐，以最大化身份相似度。为了系统性地评估跨场景鲁棒性，我们构建了一个新的基准测试，包含158个精心筛选的跨场景视频对。大量实验表明，TAVR受益于灵活的推理时视频参考，并在定量和定性上一致超越现有基线。该工作已部署到生产环境。

### [43] [Training-Free Tunnel Defect Inspection and Engineering Interpretation via Visual Recalibration and Entity Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27928)
*Shipeng Liu,Liang Zhao,Dengfeng Chen,Zhanping Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出训练-自由的隧道检测框架 TunnelMIND，通过密集视觉一致性校准语言引导的缺陷提议，生成结构化缺陷实体（包含类别、位置、几何、严重程度和上下文属性），并在可见光、GPR 和道路缺陷任务上分别达到 0.68、0.78、0.72 的 F1 分数，实现从粗粒度定位到结构化工程评估的跨越。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有训练-自由的基础模型管道通常仅生成粗粒度的开放词汇提议，难以直接用于干扰严重的隧道场景，缺乏可直接支持缺陷定位、测量、严重程度分级和工程文档编制的结构化输出。

Method: 提出训练-自由框架 TunnelMIND：(1) 在推理时通过密集视觉一致性重新校准语言引导缺陷提议的空间支撑，将粗语义锚点转换为更可靠的提示以应对隧道特定的难负样本；(2) 将生成的掩码进一步重构为带有类别、位置、几何、严重程度和上下文属性的结构化缺陷实体；(3) 在专家知识约束下，将结构化实体映射为基于检索的解释和工程可读的报告。

Result: 在可见光、GPR 和道路缺陷三个任务上，TunnelMIND 的 F1 分数分别达到 0.68、0.78 和 0.72。

Conclusion: TunnelMIND 证明训练-自由的隧道检测可以从粗粒度定位迈向用于工程评估的结构化缺陷证据。

Original Abstract: Tunnel inspection requires outputs that can support defect localization, measurement, severity grading, and engineering documentation. Existing training-free foundation-model pipelines usually stop at coarse open-vocabulary proposals, which are difficult to use directly in interference-heavy tunnel scenes. We propose a training-free framework TunnelMIND. Specifically, language-guided defect proposals are not treated as final outputs; instead, their spatial support is recalibrated at inference time through dense visual consistency, so that coarse semantic anchors can be transformed into more reliable prompts under tunnel-specific hard negatives. The resulting masks are further reconstructed into structured defect entities with category, location, geometry, severity, and context attributes, which are then mapped to retrieval-grounded explanation and engineering-readable report generation under expert knowledge constraints. On visible, GPR, and road defect tasks, TunnelMIND achieves F1 scores of 0.68, 0.78, and 0.72, respectively. Overall, TunnelMIND shows that training-free tunnel inspection can move beyond coarse localization toward structured defect evidence for engineering assessment.

中文摘要翻译: 隧道检测需要能够支持缺陷定位、测量、严重程度分级和工程文档编制的输出。现有的训练-自由基础模型管道通常止步于粗粒度的开放词汇提议，难以直接用于干扰严重的隧道场景。我们提出了一种训练-自由框架 TunnelMIND。具体而言，语言引导的缺陷提议不被视为最终输出；相反，在推理时通过密集视觉一致性对其空间支撑进行重新校准，从而将粗语义锚点在隧道特定难负样本下转化为更可靠的提示。由此产生的掩码进一步重构为带有类别、位置、几何、严重程度和上下文属性的结构化缺陷实体，然后在专家知识约束下映射到基于检索的解释和工程可读的报告生成。在可见光、探地雷达和道路缺陷任务上，TunnelMIND 分别取得了 0.68、0.78 和 0.72 的 F1 分数。总体而言，TunnelMIND 表明，训练-自由的隧道检测可以从粗粒度定位迈向用于工程评估的结构化缺陷证据。

### [44] [Dynamic Cluster Data Sampling for Efficient and Long-Tail-Aware Vision-Language Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27932)
*Mingliang Liang,Zhuoran Liu,Arjen P. de Vries,Martha Larson*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出动态聚类采样方法(DynamiCS)，通过下采样大数据簇、上采样小数据簇来平衡视觉语言模型预训练数据中的长尾概念分布，在降低计算成本的同时提升长尾概念的表现性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有高效预训练方法在采样数据时可能过度移除稀有概念，导致长尾概念在训练数据中代表性不足，无法被有效学习。

Method: 提出动态聚类采样(DynamiCS)：在每个epoch动态地对数据聚类，对大数据簇进行下采样，对小数据簇进行上采样，保持语义簇的相对顺序并强调长尾概念。

Result: DynamiCS降低了VLM训练的计算成本，并且在长尾概念上取得了性能优势。

Conclusion: 动态采样对VLM训练至关重要，所提出的聚类缩放方法优于仅扁平化语义分布的现有方法。

Original Abstract: The computational cost of training a vision-language model (VLM) can be reduced by sampling the training data. Previous work on efficient VLM pre-training has pointed to the importance of semantic data balance, adjusting the distribution of topics in the data to improve VLM accuracy. However, existing efficient pre-training approaches may disproportionately remove rare concepts from the training corpus. As a result, \emph{long-tail concepts} remain insufficiently represented in the training data and are not effectively captured during training. In this work, we introduce a \emph{dynamic cluster-based sampling approach (DynamiCS)} that downsamples large clusters of data and upsamples small ones. The approach is dynamic in that it applies sampling at each epoch. We first show the importance of dynamic sampling for VLM training. Then, we demonstrate the advantage of our cluster-scaling approach, which maintains the relative order of semantic clusters in the data and emphasizes the long-tail. This approach contrasts with current work, which focuses only on flattening the semantic distribution of the data. Our experiments show that DynamiCS reduces the computational cost of VLM training and provides a performance advantage for long-tail concepts.

中文摘要翻译: 训练视觉语言模型(VLM)的计算成本可以通过对训练数据进行采样来降低。先前关于高效VLM预训练的工作指出了语义数据平衡的重要性，即调整数据中主题的分布以提高VLM的准确性。然而，现有的高效预训练方法可能会不成比例地移除训练语料中的稀有概念。因此，长尾概念在训练数据中的代表性仍然不足，无法在训练过程中被有效捕获。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种动态聚类采样方法(DynamiCS)，该方法对大数据簇进行下采样，对小数据簇进行上采样。该方法是动态的，因为它会在每个epoch进行采样。我们首先展示了动态采样对VLM训练的重要性。然后，我们展示了聚类缩放方法的优势，该方法保持数据中语义簇的相对顺序并强调长尾概念。这种方法与当前仅关注扁平化数据语义分布的工作形成对比。我们的实验表明，DynamiCS降低了VLM训练的计算成本，并为长尾概念提供了性能优势。

Original Abstract: Due to the scarcity of large-scale in-the-wild triplet data and the improper use of masks, the performance of video virtual try-on models remains limited. In this paper, we first introduce **TripVVT-10K**, the largest and most diverse in-the-wild triplet dataset to date, providing explicit video-level cross-garment supervision that existing video datasets lack. Compared to state-of-the-art academic and commercial systems, TripVVT achieves superior video quality and garment fidelity while markedly improving generalization to challenging in-the-wild videos. ### [46] [ClimateVID -- Social Media Videos Analysis and Challenges Involved](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27968)
*Shiqi Xu,Moritz Burmester,Katharina Prasse,Isaac Bravo,Stefanie Walter,Margret Keuper*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两种分析策略：(1) 利用VideoChatGPT、PandaGPT和VideoLLaVA等VLM进行零样本图像分类，并以逐帧CLIP图像分类为基线进行对比；(2) 将聚类问题建模为最小成本多割问题，以无监督方式挖掘视觉模式。

(2) By treating clustering as a minimum cost multicut problem, we aim to uncover insightful patterns in an unsupervised manner. For both analysis strategies, we provide extensive evaluations and practical guidance to practitioners. While VLMs are currently not able to detect climate change specific classes, the clustering results are distinct visual frames. %Given that VLMs are not currently capable to grasp the climate change discourse, we focus the clustering evaluation of image embedding models. Code available at https://github.com/KathPra/ClimateVID.git.

### [47] [Echo-α: Large Agentic Multimodal Reasoning Model for Ultrasound Interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28011)
*Jing Zhang,Wentao Jiang,Tao Huang,Zhiwei Wang,Jianxin Liu,Jian Chen,Ping Ye,Gang Wang,Zengmao Wang,Bo Du,Dacheng Tao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Echo-α是一个面向超声影像解读的智能体多模态推理模型，通过调用和推理框架统一了专用检测器的强定位能力与多模态大模型的灵活推理能力，在肾脏和乳腺超声数据集上同时提升了病灶定位和诊断的准确率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法在超声影像解读中存在能力割裂：专用检测器定位强但推理弱，多模态大模型推理灵活但在专业医学领域定位能力不足。Echo-α旨在统一这两种优势，实现既精准定位又具备临床推理能力的超声AI系统。

Method: Echo-α采用invoke-and-reason框架，通过九任务监督课程学习训练模型协调器官级检测器输出并整合全局视觉上下文；随后采用序列强化学习在不同奖励权衡下进行精调，得到用于病灶锚定的Echo-α-Grounding和用于最终诊断的Echo-α-Diagnosis。

Result: 在多中心肾脏和乳腺超声基准上，Echo-α在定位和诊断任务上均优于基线方法。跨中心测试中，Echo-α-Grounding在肾脏/乳腺超声上达到56.73%/43.78%的F1@0.5，Echo-α-Diagnosis达到74.90%/49.20%的总体准确率。

Conclusion: 智能体多模态推理能够将专用检测器的输出转化为可验证的临床证据，为构建更准确、可解释且可迁移的超声AI系统提供了实用路径。

Original Abstract: Ultrasound interpretation requires both precise lesion localization and holistic clinical reasoning, yet existing methods typically excel at only one of these capabilities: specialized detectors offer strong localization but limited reasoning, whereas multimodal large language models (MLLMs) provide flexible reasoning but weak grounding in specialized medical domains. We present Echo-α, an agentic multimodal reasoning model for ultrasound interpretation that unifies these strengths within an invoke-and-reason framework. Echo-α is trained to coordinate organ-specific detector outputs, integrate them with global visual context, and convert the resulting evidence into grounded diagnostic decisions beyond detector-only inference. This behavior is established through a nine-task supervised curriculum and then refined by sequential reinforcement learning under different reward trade-offs, yielding Echo-α-Grounding for lesion anchoring and Echo-α-Diagnosis for final diagnosis. On multi-center renal and breast ultrasound benchmarks, Echo-α outperforms competitive baselines on both grounding and diagnosis. In particular, on cross-center test sets, Echo-α-Grounding attains 56.73%/43.78% F1@0.5 and Echo- α-Diagnosis reaches 74.90%/49.20% overall accuracy on renal/breast ultrasound. These results suggest that agentic multimodal reasoning can turn specialized detectors into verifiable clinical evidence, offering a practical route toward ultrasound AI systems that are more accurate, interpretable, and transferable. The repository is at https://github.com/MiliLab/Echo-Alpha.

中文摘要翻译: 超声影像解读既需要精确的病灶定位，也需要整体的临床推理，然而现有方法通常仅擅长其中一种能力：专用检测器定位能力强但推理能力有限，而多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）推理灵活但在专业医学领域的定位能力不足。我们提出Echo-α，一种面向超声影像解读的智能体多模态推理模型，通过调用和推理框架统一了这两种优势。Echo-α经过训练能够协调器官级检测器的输出，将其与全局视觉上下文整合，并将所得证据转化为超越检测器单独推理的基于证据的诊断决策。这一行为通过九任务监督课程学习建立，随后通过不同奖励权衡下的序列强化学习进行精调，得到用于病灶锚定的Echo-α-Grounding和用于最终诊断的Echo-α-Diagnosis。在多中心肾脏和乳腺超声基准上，Echo-α在定位和诊断任务上均优于竞争性基线方法。特别是在跨中心测试集上，Echo-α-Grounding在肾脏/乳腺超声上分别达到56.73%/43.78%的F1@0.5，Echo-α-Diagnosis达到74.90%/49.20%的总体准确率。这些结果表明，智能体多模态推理能够将专用检测器输出转化为可验证的临床证据，为构建更准确、可解释且可迁移的超声AI系统提供了实用路径。代码仓库地址：https://github.com/MiliLab/Echo-Alpha。

### [48] [Faster 3D Gaussian Splatting Convergence via Structure-Aware Densification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28016)
*Linjie Lyu,Ayush Tewari,Jianchun Chen,Thomas Leimkühler,Christian Theobalt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种结构感知的3D高斯溅射密集化框架，通过多尺度频率分析和各向异性分裂策略，解决传统方法在高频区域的模糊或过度密集问题，实现更快收敛和更优重建质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准3D高斯溅射的自适应密度控制依赖屏幕空间位置梯度，无法区分几何错位与频率混叠，导致高频纹理过模糊或过度密集化。

Method: 提出结构感知密集化框架，核心包括：(1) 多尺度频率分析——结合结构张量与拉普拉斯尺度空间分析，估计每个像素的主导频率；(2) 定义频率违反度量η——逐高斯、逐轴地指示原始体素是否欠解析局部纹理细节；(3) 各向异性分裂——对η高的轴计算分裂因子以更好解析局部频率内容；(4) 多视角一致性准则——聚合多视角下的η观测值。

Result: 在标准基准上达到更优的重建质量，尤其在高频区域；通过更早更快地执行密集化，跳过了基线方法所需的冗长迭代密集化阶段，实现了显著更快的收敛速度。

Conclusion: 通过结构感知的密集化策略，有效区分了几何误差与频率欠采样，各向异性分裂能更高效地匹配局部纹理复杂度，从而在加速收敛的同时提升重建保真度。

Original Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting has emerged as a powerful scene representation for real-time novel-view synthesis. However, its standard adaptive density control relies on screen-space positional gradients, which do not distinguish between geometric misplacement and frequency aliasing, often leading to either over-blurred high-frequency textures or inefficient over-densification. We present a structure-aware densification framework. Our key insight is that the decision to subdivide a Gaussian should be driven by an explicit comparison between its projected screen-space extent and the local structure of the texture it seeks to represent. We introduce a multi-scale frequency analysis combining structure tensors with Laplacian scale space analysis to estimate the dominant frequency at each pixel, enabling robust supervision across varying texture scales. Based on this analysis, we define $η$, a per-Gaussian, per-axis frequency violation metric that indicates when a primitive may be under-resolving local texture details. Unlike methods that perform isotropic splitting (e.g., splitting each Gaussian into two smaller ones with uniform shape), our approach performs anisotropic splitting. For each axis with high $η$, we compute a split factor to better resolve the local frequency content. We further introduce a multiview consistency criterion that aggregates $η$ observations across multiple views. By performing densification early and faster, we skip the lengthy iterative densification phases required by baseline methods and achieve significantly faster convergence. Experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that our method also achieves superior reconstruction quality, particularly in high-frequency regions.

中文摘要翻译: 3D高斯溅射已成为实时新视角合成的一种强大场景表示方法。然而，其标准的自适应密度控制依赖于屏幕空间位置梯度，无法区分几何错位与频率混叠，常常导致高频纹理过度模糊或低效的过度密集化。我们提出了一种结构感知的密集化框架。我们的关键洞察是：细分一个高斯体的决策应基于其投影屏幕空间范围与其试图表示的纹理局部结构之间的显式比较。我们引入了一种多尺度频率分析，将结构张量与拉普拉斯尺度空间分析相结合，以估计每个像素的主导频率，从而实现对不同纹理尺度的鲁棒监督。基于该分析，我们定义了η——一种逐高斯、逐轴的频率违反度量，用于指示某个原始体素是否欠解析局部纹理细节。与执行各向同性分裂的方法（例如，将每个高斯体分裂为两个形状均匀的更小高斯体）不同，我们的方法执行各向异性分裂。对于每个η高的轴，我们计算一个分裂因子，以更好地解析局部频率内容。我们进一步引入了一种多视角一致性准则，聚合来自多个视角的η观测值。通过更早、更快地执行密集化，我们跳过了基线方法所需的冗长迭代密集化阶段，并实现了显著更快的收敛速度。在标准基准上的实验表明，我们的方法在重建质量上也达到了更优的效果，尤其是在高频区域。

</details>


### [49] [TAFA-GSGC: Group-wise Scalable Point Cloud Geometry Compression with Progressive Residual Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28045)
*Xiumei Li,Alexander Kopte,André Kaup*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TAFA-GSGC是一种可扩展的点云几何编解码器，通过分层残差细化与通道组熵编码以及目标对齐特征聚合模块，实现单个比特流和单个模型的多质量解码，支持最多9个可解码质量层级，相比PCGCv2获得平均-4.99%（D1）和-5.92%（D2）的BD-Rate节省。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有学习型编解码器通常针对单一率失真点优化，实现率自适应需要重新编码或维护多个比特流，代价高昂，因此需要一种可扩展的编解码方案。

Method: 提出TAFA-GSGC框架，结合分层残差细化与通道组熵编码，并引入目标对齐特征聚合（Target-Aligned Feature Aggregation）模块，以减少增强残差中的跨层冗余。

Result: 支持最多9个质量层级，随子比特流增加实现单调质量提升；与基线PCGCv2相比，达到可比且略优的率失真性能，BD-Rate在D1上节省-4.99%，在D2上节省-5.92%。

Conclusion: TAFA-GSGC在保持强压缩效率的同时，实现了单比特流单模型的多质量可扩展解码，有效解决了率自适应传输中的成本问题。

Original Abstract: Scalable compression is essential for bandwidth-adaptive transmission, yet most learned codecs are optimized for a fixed rate-distortion point, making rate adaptation costly due to re-encoding or maintaining multiple bitstreams. In this work, we propose TAFA-GSGC, a scalable learned point cloud geometry codec that enables multi-quality decoding from a single bitstream and a single trained model. TAFA-GSGC combines layered residual refinement with channel-group entropy coding, and introduces Target-Aligned Feature Aggregation module to reduce cross-layer redundancy in enhancement residuals. Our framework supports up to 9 decodable quality levels with monotonic quality improvement as more subbitstreams are received, while maintaining strong compression efficiency. Compared with the baseline PCGCv2, TAFA-GSGC attains comparable and slightly better RD performance, achieving average BD-Rate savings of -4.99% in D1 and -5.92% in D2.

中文摘要翻译: 可扩展压缩对于带宽自适应传输至关重要，然而大多数学习型编解码器针对固定的率失真点进行优化，导致率自适应因需重新编码或维护多个比特流而代价高昂。在这项工作中，我们提出了TAFA-GSGC，一种可扩展的学习型点云几何编解码器，能够从单个比特流和单个训练模型中实现多质量解码。TAFA-GSGC将分层残差细化与通道组熵编码相结合，并引入了目标对齐特征聚合模块以减少增强残差中的跨层冗余。我们的框架支持多达9个可解码质量层级，随着更多子比特流被接收，质量单调提升，同时保持强大的压缩效率。与基线PCGCv2相比，TAFA-GSGC达到了可比且略优的率失真性能，在D1和D2指标上分别实现了平均-4.99%和-5.92%的BD-Rate节省。

### [50] [3D Reconstruction Techniques in the Manufacturing Domain: Applications, Research Opportunities and Use Cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28064)
*Chialoon Cheng,Kaijun liu,Zhiyang Liu,Marcelo H Ang*

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了制造业应用中三维重建技术的发展现状，涵盖传统方法与新兴深度学习方法，指出统一三维重建框架的研究空白，并基于106篇文献将技术分为数据采集、点云生成、后处理与应用三类，其中非接触式方法（特别是结构光扫描和立体视觉）已被广泛采用，深度学习显著提升了重建精度与速度。

Method: 采用系统性文献综述方法，对106篇近期出版物进行分类分析，将三维重建技术归纳为三个主要类别：数据采集、点云生成、后处理与应用。对各类方法在制造业中的采用情况、性能表现和应用分布进行了统计分析。

Result: 非接触式方法（特别是结构光扫描和立体视觉）在制造业中广泛采用，47%的调研应用聚焦于质量检测。深度学习在特征提取和匹配方面显著提升了重建精度和处理速度。应用分布为：设计与开发13%、加工8、工艺17%、装配22%、质量检测40%。当前技术在受控环境中可达亚毫米级精度。

Conclusion: 当前三维重建技术呈现向混合系统发展的趋势，即结合多种传感器类型和处理方法以克服单一技术的局限性。本文为理解制造业三维重建的当前能力和未来方向提供了结构化框架。

Original Abstract: This comprehensive review examines the evolution and the current state of the art in three-dimensional (3D) reconstruction techniques in manufacturing applications. The analysis covers both traditional approaches and emerging deep learning methods, showing a critical research gap in unified 3d reconstruction frameworks. Through systematic review of 106 recent publications, we classify reconstruction techniques into three primary categories: data acquisition, point cloud generation, post-processing and applications. Non-contact methods, particularly structured light scanning and stereo vision, have shown significant adoption in manufacturing, with 47% of surveyed applications focusing on quality inspection. The integration of deep learning has enhanced reconstruction accuracy and processing speed, particularly in feature extraction and matching. Key applications span design and development (13%), machining (8%), process (17%), assembly (22%), and quality inspection (40%). While current technologies achieve sub-millimeter accuracy in controlled environments, challenges persist in handling reflective surfaces and dynamic environments. Our findings indicate a trend toward hybrid systems combining multiple sensor types and processing methods to overcome individual limitations. This survey provides a structured framework for understanding current capabilities and future directions in manufacturing-focused 3D reconstruction.

### [51] [AesRM: Improving Video Aesthetics with Expert-Level Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28078)
*Yujin Han,Yujie Wei,Yefei He,Xinyu Liu,Tianle Li,Zichao Yu,Andi Han,Shiwei Zhang,Tingyu Weng,Difan Zou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种层次化评价体系，将视频美学分解为视觉美学、视觉保真度和视觉合理性三个核心维度及15个细粒度标准，构建了专家标注偏好数据集和评估基准AesVideo-Bench，并训练了视频美学奖励模型AesRM（包括Base和CoT版本），通过三阶段渐进训练方案提升评估准确性和可解释性，最终将AesRM用于对齐视频生成模型Wan2.2，取得了明显的美学提升。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视频生成研究主要关注视觉保真度，缺乏对视频美学的系统定义和评估；此前视觉美学工作多聚焦于图像，且定义粗糙（如“视觉愉悦”），缺乏严格系统的评估标准。因此需要为视频美学建立层次化、可量化的评价体系及相应的奖励模型。

Method: (1) 提出层次化美学评价体系（VA/VF/VP）及15个细粒度标准；(2) 构建大规模专家标注偏好数据集和AesVideo-Bench基准；(3) 训练AesRM-Base（直接预测偏好）和AesRM-CoT（生成符合15条标准的思维链以增强可解释性）；(4) 设计三阶段渐进训练：原子美学能力学习→冷启动对齐结构化推理→GRPO优化；(5) 针对AesRM-CoT提出基于自一致性的思维链合成方法和基于思维链的过程奖励机制。

Result: AesRM在多个美学基准上优于基线方法，且具有更低的位偏置（position bias）和更强的鲁棒性；将Wan2.2与AesRM对齐后，相比现有美学奖励模型取得了明显的美学提升。

Conclusion: 提出的层次化视频美学评价框架和AesRM奖励模型能够有效评估和提升视频美学质量，为视频生成的美学优化提供了系统化的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Despite rapid advances in photorealistic video generation, real-world applications such as filmmaking require video aesthetics, e.g., harmonious colors and cinematic lighting, beyond visual fidelity. Prior work on visual aesthetics largely focuses on images, often reducing aesthetics to coarse definitions, e.g., visual pleasure, without a rigorous and systematic evaluation. To improve video aesthetics, we propose a hierarchical rubric that decomposes video aesthetics into three core dimensions, Visual Aesthetics (VA), Visual Fidelity (VF), and Visual Plausibility (VP), with 15 fine-grained criteria, e.g., shot composition. This framework enables a large-scale expert-annotated preference dataset and an evaluation benchmark, AesVideo-Bench, containing about 2500 video pairs with expert annotations on VA, VF, and VP. We then build a family of Video Aesthetic Reward Models (AesRM): AesRM-Base, which directly predicts pairwise preferences on these dimensions to provide efficient post-training rewards, and AesRM-CoT, which additionally generates CoT aligned with all 15 criteria to improve assessment interpretability. Specifically, we train AesRM with a three-stage progressive scheme: (1) Atomic Aesthetic Capability Learning, which strengthens AesRM's recognition of fundamental aesthetic concepts, e.g., accurately identifying centered composition; (2) Cold-Start, aligning the model with structured reasoning protocols; and (3) GRPO, further improving evaluation accuracy. To enhance AesRM-CoT, we additionally propose self-consistency-based CoT synthesis to improve CoT quality and design CoT-based process rewards during GRPO. Extensive experiments show AesRM outperforms baselines on multiple aesthetics benchmarks and is more robust, with lower position bias. Finally, we align Wan2.2 with AesRM and observe clear aesthetic gains over existing aesthetic reward models.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管逼真的视频生成技术取得了快速进展，但电影制作等实际应用不仅需要视觉保真度，还需要视频美学品质，例如和谐的色彩和电影感的灯光。先前关于视觉美学的工作主要集中在图像上，且往往将美学简化为粗糙的定义（如"视觉愉悦"），缺乏严格系统的评估。为了提升视频美学，我们提出了一个层次化评价体系，将视频美学分解为三个核心维度：视觉美学（VA）、视觉保真度（VF）和视觉合理性（VP），包含15个细粒度标准（如镜头构图）。该框架支持构建大规模专家标注偏好数据集及评估基准AesVideo-Bench，包含约2500个视频对及其专家在VA、VF和VP上的标注。在此基础上，我们构建了视频美学奖励模型家族（AesRM）：AesRM-Base直接预测这些维度上的成对偏好以提供高效的后训练奖励；AesRM-CoT则额外生成与全部15条标准对齐的思维链，以提升评估的可解释性。具体而言，我们采用三阶段渐进方案训练AesRM：（1）原子美学能力学习，增强模型对基础美学概念的识别能力（如准确定位居中构图）；（2）冷启动阶段，使模型与结构化推理协议对齐；（3）GRPO阶段，进一步提升评估准确性。为增强AesRM-CoT，我们还提出基于自一致性的思维链合成方法以提升思维链质量，并在GRPO过程中设计基于思维链的过程奖励。大量实验表明，AesRM在多个美学基准上优于基线方法，且具有更低的位偏置和更强的鲁棒性。最后，我们将Wan2.2与AesRM对齐，观察到相比于现有美学奖励模型有明显的美学提升。

</details>


### [52] [Beyond Gaussian Bottlenecks: Topologically Aligned Encoding of Vision-Transformer Feature Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28122)
*Andrew Bond,Ilkin Umut Melanlioglu,Erkut Erdem,Aykut Erdem*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出S²VAE，一种几何优先的潜在学习框架，使用Power Spherical分布的乘积作为潜在先验，在强压缩下保留3D几何与方向语义，优于传统高斯瓶颈。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视觉世界模型虽能生成合理运动，但常无法保持底层3D几何与物理一致的相机动态，关键在于潜在表示缺乏对几何结构的显式编码。

Method: 基于VGGT表示，提出一种新型变分自编码器，使用Power Spherical分布的乘积作为潜在先验，在瓶颈层显式施加超球面结构以保留方向与几何语义。

Result: 在深度估计、相机位姿恢复和点云重建任务中，几何对齐的超球面潜在表示在高压缩比下一致优于传统高斯瓶颈。

Conclusion: 潜在几何应作为物理接地视觉与世界模型的一等设计选择，几何优先的潜在学习比单纯扩大模型容量更关键。

Original Abstract: Modern visual world modeling systems increasingly rely on high-capacity architectures and large-scale data to produce plausible motion, yet they often fail to preserve underlying 3D geometry or physically consistent camera dynamics. A key limitation lies not only in model capacity, but in the latent representations used to encode geometric structure. We propose S$^2$VAE, a geometry-first latent learning framework that focuses on compressing and representing the latent 3D state of a scene, including camera motion, depth, and point-level structure, rather than modeling appearance alone. Building on representations from a Visual Geometry Grounded Transformer (VGGT), we introduce a novel type of variational autoencoder using a product of Power Spherical latent distributions, explicitly enforcing hyperspherical structure in the bottleneck to preserve directional and geometric semantics under strong compression. Across depth estimation, camera pose recovery, and point cloud reconstruction, we show that geometry-aligned hyperspherical latents consistently outperform conventional Gaussian bottlenecks, particularly in high-compression regimes. Our results highlight latent geometry as a first-class design choice for physically grounded visual and world models.

中文摘要翻译: 现代视觉世界建模系统日益依赖高容量架构和大规模数据来生成合理的运动，然而它们常常无法保持底层的3D几何或物理一致的相机动态。一个关键限制不仅在于模型容量，还在于用于编码几何结构的潜在表示。我们提出S²VAE，一种几何优先的潜在学习框架，其重点在于压缩和表示场景的潜在3D状态，包括相机运动、深度和点级结构，而非仅建模外观。基于视觉几何接地变换器（VGGT）的表示，我们引入了一种新型变分自编码器，使用Power Spherical潜在分布的乘积，在瓶颈层显式施加超球面结构，以在强压缩下保留方向和几何语义。在深度估计、相机位姿恢复和点云重建任务中，我们证明几何对齐的超球面潜在表示在高压缩比下始终优于传统高斯瓶颈。我们的结果突显出潜在几何应作为物理接地视觉和世界模型的一等设计选择。

### [53] [AdvDMD: Adversarial Reward Meets DMD For High-Quality Few-Step Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28126)
*Xu Wang,Zexian Li,Litong Gong,Tiezheng Ge,Zhijie Deng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AdvDMD，将分布匹配蒸馏（DMD）与强化学习（RL）统一融合，利用DMD2的对抗训练判别器作为奖励模型，在少步采样下实现超越教师模型的生成质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有蒸馏方法在少步采样时性能下降明显，而将RL与蒸馏结合的组合式方法引入了不必要的复杂性。需要一种无缝统一DMD蒸馏和RL的方法，以简化流程并提升少步生成质量。

Method: AdvDMD将DMD2中对抗训练的判别器作为RL的奖励模型（对生成图像给低分，对真实图像给高分），在去噪过程的中间状态和最终状态上训练判别器，并与蒸馏模型进行在线更新，从而对采样轨迹进行全面监督并缓解奖励破解。采用统一的SDE反向模拟以及DMD与RL的不同训练调度，实现更稳定高效的训练。

Result: 4步AdvDMD在DPG-Bench上超过了原始40步的SD3.5模型；在GenEval上对SD3实现了显著的性能提升；2步AdvDMD在Qwen-Image上优于TwinFlow。

Conclusion: AdvDMD通过将DMD蒸馏与RL无缝统一，在极少量采样步数下能够超越教师模型的性能，为扩散模型的高效少步生成提供了有效方案。

Original Abstract: Diffusion models offer superior generation quality at the expense of extensive sampling steps.
  Distillation methods, with Distribution Matching Distillation (DMD) as a popular example, can mitigate this issue, but performance degradation remains pronounced when sampling steps are limited.
  Reinforcement learning (RL) has been leveraged to improve the few-step generation quality during distillation, with the potential to even surpass the performance of the teacher model. However, existing approaches are combinatorial in nature, merely integrating an RL process with the distillation process, which introduces unnecessary complexities. To address this gap, we propose AdvDMD, a method that seamlessly unifies DMD distillation and RL.
  Specifically, AdvDMD employs the adversarially trained discriminator from DMD2 as the reward model, which assigns low scores to generated images and high scores to real ones.
  It is trained on both intermediate and final states of the denoising process and updated online with the distilled model, enabling a holistic supervision of the sampling trajectories and mitigating reward hacking.
  We adopt a unified SDE backward simulation and a different training schedule for DMD and RL to enable a more stable and efficient training.
  Experimental results demonstrate that the 4-step AdvDMD outperforms the original 40-step model for SD3.5 on DPG-Bench, while achieving significant performance gains for SD3 on the GenEval.
  On Qwen-Image, our 2-step AdvDMD achieves superior performance over TwinFlow.

中文摘要翻译: 扩散模型以大量的采样步骤为代价，提供了优越的生成质量。蒸馏方法（以分布匹配蒸馏DMD为典型代表）可以缓解这一问题，但当采样步骤受限时，性能下降仍然明显。强化学习已被用于在蒸馏过程中提升少步生成质量，甚至有潜力超越教师模型的性能。然而，现有方法本质上是组合式的，仅仅是将RL过程与蒸馏过程进行整合，引入了不必要的复杂性。为解决这一空白，我们提出了AdvDMD，一种将DMD蒸馏与RL无缝统一的方法。具体来说，AdvDMD采用DMD2中对抗训练的判别器作为奖励模型，该模型对生成的图像给予低分，对真实图像给予高分。该判别器在去噪过程的中间状态和最终状态上进行训练，并与蒸馏模型进行在线更新，从而实现对采样轨迹的全面监督并缓解奖励破解。我们采用统一的SDE反向模拟以及DMD与RL的不同训练调度，以实现更稳定和高效的训练。实验结果表明，在DPG-Bench上，4步AdvDMD在SD3.5上优于原始的40步模型，同时在GenEval上对SD3实现了显著的性能提升。在Qwen-Image上，我们的2步AdvDMD取得了优于TwinFlow的性能。

</details>


### [54] [3D-ReGen: A Unified 3D Geometry Regeneration Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28134)
*Geon Yeong Park,Roman Shapovalov,Rakesh Ranjan,Jong Chul Ye,Andrea Vedaldi,Thu Nguyen-Phuoc*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 3D-ReGen是一个基于初始3D形状条件的3D再生器，通过VecSet新条件机制和自监督预文任务，支持3D增强、重建和编辑等多种任务，在可控3D生成中达到最先进性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有3D生成器大多采用“一次性”方式从文本或图像生成3D对象，控制能力有限。作者希望引入一种基于初始3D形状条件的再生框架，以支持更灵活、可控的3D生成任务，如增强、重建和编辑。

Method: 提出3D-ReGen，核心创新包括：(1) 基于VecSet的新型条件机制，使再生器能够以一致的细粒度细节更新或改进输入几何；(2) 通过自监督预文任务和数据增强，从现成的3D数据集中学习广泛适用的再生先验，无需额外标注。

Original Abstract: We consider the problem of regenerating 3D objects from 2D images and initial 3D shapes. Most 3D generators operate in a one-shot fashion, converting text or images to a 3D object with limited controllability. We introduce instead 3D-ReGen, a 3D regenerator that is conditioned on an initial 3D shape. This conceptually simple formulation allows us to support numerous useful tasks, including 3D enhancement, reconstruction, and editing. 3D-ReGen uses a new conditioning mechanism based on VecSet, which allows the regenerator to update or improve the input geometry with consistent fine-grained details. 3D-ReGen learns a widely applicable regeneration prior from off-the-shelf 3D datasets via self-supervised pretext tasks and augmentations, without additional annotations. We evaluate both the geometric consistency and fine-grained quality of 3D-ReGen, achieving state-of-the-art performance in controllable 3D generation across several tasks.

中文摘要翻译: 本文研究了从2D图像和初始3D形状再生3D对象的问题。大多数3D生成器采用一次性生成方式，将文本或图像转换为3D对象，但其可控性有限。我们提出了3D-ReGen，一种以初始3D形状为条件的3D再生器。这一概念上简洁的公式使我们能够支持众多有用的任务，包括3D增强、重建和编辑。3D-ReGen使用了一种基于VecSet的新型条件机制，使再生器能够以一致的细粒度细节更新或改进输入几何。3D-ReGen通过自监督预文任务和数据增强，从现成的3D数据集中学习广泛适用的再生先验，无需额外标注。我们在几何一致性和细粒度质量两方面评估了3D-ReGen，在多个可控3D生成任务上达到了最先进性能。

### [55] [PhyCo: Learning Controllable Physical Priors for Generative Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28169)
*Sriram Narayanan,Ziyu Jiang,Srinivasa Narasimhan,Manmohan Chandraker*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PhyCo是一个将连续、可解释且物理可控信号引入视频生成的框架，通过大规模物理仿真数据集、基于物理属性图的ControlNet微调以及VLM引导的奖励优化，显著提升了生成视频的物理一致性，且推理时无需仿真器或几何重建。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视频扩散模型在视觉外观上表现出色，但生成的视频往往存在物体飘移、碰撞无真实反弹、材质响应与物理属性不符等物理不一致问题，缺乏对物理行为的可控生成能力。

Method: (i) 构建包含10万以上不同摩擦、恢复系数、形变和力参数的光真实感仿真视频数据集；(ii) 使用以像素对齐的物理属性图为条件的ControlNet，对预训练扩散模型进行物理监督的微调；(iii) 利用微调的视觉-语言模型对生成视频进行目标物理查询评估，并提供可微分的奖励反馈进行优化。

Result: 在Physics-IQ基准测试上，PhyCo显著提升了物理真实性，超越了多个强基线模型；用户研究进一步证实了其对物理属性更清晰、更忠实的控制能力。

Conclusion: PhyCo提供了一条可扩展的路径，能够构建物理一致、可控的生成式视频模型，并且其泛化能力超越了合成训练环境的限制。

Original Abstract: Modern video diffusion models excel at appearance synthesis but still struggle with physical consistency: objects drift, collisions lack realistic rebound, and material responses seldom match their underlying properties. We present PhyCo, a framework that introduces continuous, interpretable, and physically grounded control into video generation. Our approach integrates three key components: (i) a large-scale dataset of over 100K photorealistic simulation videos where friction, restitution, deformation, and force are systematically varied across diverse scenarios; (ii) physics-supervised fine-tuning of a pretrained diffusion model using a ControlNet conditioned on pixel-aligned physical property maps; and (iii) VLM-guided reward optimization, where a fine-tuned vision-language model evaluates generated videos with targeted physics queries and provides differentiable feedback. This combination enables a generative model to produce physically consistent and controllable outputs through variations in physical attributes-without any simulator or geometry reconstruction at inference. On the Physics-IQ benchmark, PhyCo significantly improves physical realism over strong baselines, and human studies confirm clearer and more faithful control over physical attributes. Our results demonstrate a scalable path toward physically consistent, controllable generative video models that generalize beyond synthetic training environments.

中文摘要翻译: 现代视频扩散模型在外观合成方面表现出色，但在物理一致性方面仍然存在困难：物体漂移、碰撞缺乏真实的反弹，以及材质响应很少与它们的内在属性相匹配。我们提出了PhyCo，一个将连续、可解释且具有物理基础的控制引入视频生成的框架。我们的方法集成了三个关键组件：(i) 一个包含超过10万个光真实感仿真视频的大规模数据集，其中摩擦、恢复系数、形变和力在不同场景中系统地变化；(ii) 使用以像素对齐的物理属性图为条件的ControlNet，对预训练扩散模型进行物理监督的微调；(iii) 视觉-语言模型（VLM）引导的奖励优化，其中微调的视觉-语言模型通过针对性的物理查询评估生成的视频，并提供可微分的反馈。这种组合使得生成模型能够通过物理属性的变化产生物理一致且可控的输出——在推理时无需任何仿真器或几何重建。在Physics-IQ基准测试上，PhyCo相对于强基线模型显著提升了物理真实感，用户研究也证实了对物理属性更清晰、更忠实的控制。我们的结果展示了一条可扩展的路径，能够构建物理一致、可控的生成式视频模型，并且其泛化能力超越了合成训练环境的限制。

</details>


### [56] [AEGIS: A Holistic Benchmark for Evaluating Forensic Analysis of AI-Generated Academic Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28177)
*Bo Zhang,Tzu-Yen Ma,Zichen Tang,Junpeng Ding,Zirui Wang,Yizhuo Zhao,Peilin Gao,Zijie Xi,Zixin Ding,Haiyang Sun,Haocheng Gao,Yuan Liu,Liangjia Wang,Yiling Huang,Yujie Wang,Yuyue Zhang,Ronghui Xi,Yuanze Li,Jiacheng Liu,Zhongjun Yang,Haihong E*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AEGIS是一个针对AI生成学术图像取证进行全面评估的基准，涵盖7大学科类别、39个细分子类型、4种伪造策略及25种生成模型，揭示了当前检测模型在学术图像取证中的根本局限。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基准无法充分反映学术图像取证的复杂性和挑战，缺乏对多样化伪造策略和多维度评估的综合考量，因此需要构建一个更全面、更贴近真实学术场景的基准来系统评估AI生成学术图像的取证能力。

Method: 构建了覆盖7大学科类别（39个细分子类型）的基准数据集；模拟4种主流学术伪造策略，使用25种生成模型生成图像；从检测、推理、定位三个维度设计评估任务；对25个多模态大语言模型、9个专家检测模型和1个统一多模态理解与生成模型进行全面评估。

Result: GPT-5.1总体性能仅达48.80%；11种生成模型产生的图像平均取证准确率低于50%；专家模型定位精度有限（IoU 30.09%）；多模态大语言模型在文本伪影识别上达84.74%准确率，专家检测模型在二分类真伪检测上峰值达79.54%。

Conclusion: AEGIS揭示了当前学术图像取证领域取证能力落后于生成技术发展的根本局限，所有模型在该基准上表现均不理想，表明学术图像取证仍需重大突破。

Original Abstract: We introduce AEGIS, A holistic benchmark for Evaluating forensic analysis of AI-Generated academic ImageS. Compared to existing benchmarks, AEGIS features three key advances: (1) Domain-Specific Complexity: covering seven academic categories with 39 fine-grained subtypes, exposing intrinsic forensic difficulty, where even GPT-5.1 reaches 48.80% overall performance and expert models achieve only limited localization accuracy (IoU 30.09%); (2) Diverse Forgery Simulations: modeling four prevalent academic forgery strategies across 25 generative models, with 11 yielding average forensic accuracy below 50%, showing that forensics lag behind generative advances; and (3) Multi-Dimensional Forensic Evaluation: jointly assessing detection, reasoning, and localization, revealing complementary strengths between model families, with multimodal large language models (MLLMs) at 84.74% accuracy in textual artifact recognition and expert detectors peaking at 79.54% accuracy in binary authenticity detection. By evaluating 25 leading MLLMs, nine expert models, and one unified multimodal understanding and generation model, AEGIS serves as a diagnostic testbed exposing fundamental limitations in academic image forensics.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了AEGIS，一个用于评估AI生成学术图像取证分析的整体性基准。与现有基准相比，AEGIS具有三个关键进步：（1）领域特异性复杂度：覆盖七大学术类别，包含39个细分子类型，揭示了内在的取证难度——即便是GPT-5.1的整体性能也仅为48.80%，专家模型仅能达到有限的定位精度（IoU 30.09%）；（2）多样化伪造仿真：模拟了跨越25种生成模型的四种主流学术伪造策略，其中11种生成模型产生的图像平均取证准确率低于50%，表明取证能力落后于生成技术的发展；（3）多维度取证评估：联合评估检测、推理和定位能力，揭示了不同模型家族间的互补优势——多模态大语言模型在文本伪影识别上准确率达84.74%，专家检测模型在二分类真伪检测上峰值准确率达79.54%。通过对25个领先的多模态大语言模型、9个专家检测模型和1个统一多模态理解与生成模型进行评估，AEGIS作为一个诊断性测试平台，揭示了学术图像取证中的根本性局限。

### [57] [Stop Holding Your Breath: CT-Informed Gaussian Splatting for Dynamic Bronchoscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28179)
*Andrea Dunn Beltran,Daniel Rho,Aarav Mehta,Xinqi Xiong,Raúl San José Estépar,Ron Alterovitz,Marc Niethammer,Roni Sengupta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需屏气协议的支气管镜导航方法，通过患者特异性呼吸建模和网格锚定的高斯溅射框架，直接从内窥镜RGB图像推断呼吸相位，实现了呼吸周期内的连续变形感知重建，定位精度达1.22mm。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 呼吸运动导致气道变形5-20mm，造成CT与体内解剖结构不一致，限制了支气管镜导航的定位精度。现有方法依赖屏气协议来匹配术中解剖结构与静态CT，但屏气协议难以复现且扰乱临床工作流程。

Method: 利用规划时已采集的配对吸气-呼气CT扫描，通过配准将呼吸运动简化为每帧单个标量呼吸相位；将该表示嵌入网格锚定的高斯溅射框架中，使用轻量级估计器直接从内窥镜RGB图像推断呼吸相位，实现无需屏气或外部传感的连续变形感知重建。

Result: 在RESPIRE模拟数据集上，该方法实现了几何保真的重建，训练速度快20倍以上，目标定位精度达1.22mm（在临床相关的3mm容差范围内），优于未约束的单CT基线方法。

Conclusion: 通过患者特异性呼吸建模和呼吸相位推断，消除了屏气协议的需求，在保证高定位精度的同时显著提升了训练效率，有望改善支气管镜导航的临床工作流程。

Original Abstract: Bronchoscopic navigation relies on registering endoscopic video to a preoperative CT scan, but respiratory motion deforms the airway by 5-20 mm, creating CT-to-body divergence that limits localization accuracy. In practice, this is mitigated through breath-hold protocols, which attempt to match the intraoperative anatomy to a static CT, but are difficult to reproduce and disrupt clinical workflow. We propose to eliminate the need for breath-hold protocols by leveraging patient-specific respiratory modeling. Paired inhale-exhale CT scans, already acquired for planning, implicitly define the patient-specific deformation space of the breathing airway. By registering these scans, we reduce respiratory motion to a single scalar breathing phase per frame, constraining all reconstructions to anatomically observed configurations. We embed this representation within a mesh-anchored Gaussian splatting framework, where a lightweight estimator infers breathing phase directly from endoscopic RGB, enabling continuous, deformation-aware reconstruction throughout the respiratory cycle without breath-holds or external sensing. To enable quantitative evaluation, we introduce RESPIRE, a physically grounded bronchoscopy simulation pipeline with per-frame ground truth for geometry, pose, breathing phase, and deformation. Experiments on RESPIRE show that our approach achieves geometrically faithful reconstruction, over 20x faster training, and 1.22 mm target localization accuracy (within the 3mm clinically relevant tolerances) outperforming unconstrained single-CT baselines. Please check out our website for additional visuals: https://asdunnbe.github.io/RESPIRE/

中文摘要翻译: 支气管镜导航依赖于将内窥镜视频与术前CT扫描进行配准，但呼吸运动会导致气道变形5-20mm，产生CT与体内解剖结构之间的偏差，从而限制了定位精度。在实践中，这一问题通过屏气协议来缓解，该方法试图使术中解剖结构与静态CT相匹配，但屏气协议难以复现且会扰乱临床工作流程。我们提出通过利用患者特异性呼吸建模来消除对屏气协议的需求。规划阶段已采集的配对吸气-呼气CT扫描隐含地定义了呼吸气道的患者特异性变形空间。通过配准这些扫描，我们将呼吸运动简化为每帧一个标量呼吸相位，将所有重建约束在解剖学上可观测的构型内。我们将这一表示嵌入到网格锚定的高斯溅射框架中，其中轻量级估计器直接从内窥镜RGB图像推断呼吸相位，从而在整个呼吸周期内实现无需屏气或外部传感的连续变形感知重建。为支持定量评估，我们引入了RESPIRE——一个物理基础的支气管镜模拟管道，提供每帧的几何、姿态、呼吸相位和变形真值。在RESPIRE上的实验表明，我们的方法实现了几何保真的重建，训练速度快20倍以上，目标定位精度达1.22mm（在3mm临床相关容差范围内），优于未约束的单CT基线方法。更多可视化结果请访问我们的网站：https://asdunnbe.github.io/RESPIRE/

### [58] [Visual Generation in the New Era: An Evolution from Atomic Mapping to Agentic World Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28185)
*Keming Wu,Zuhao Yang,Kaichen Zhang,Shizun Wang,Haowei Zhu,Sicong Leng,Zhongyu Yang,Qijie Wang,Sudong Wang,Ziting Wang,Zili Wang,Hui Zhang,Haonan Wang,Hang Zhou,Yifan Pu,Xingxuan Li,Fangneng Zhan,Bo Li,Lidong Bing,Yuxin Song,Ziwei Liu,Wenhu Chen,Jingdong Wang,Xinchao Wang,Xiaojuan Qi,Shijian Lu,Bin Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出视觉生成领域应从外观合成转向智能视觉生成，并引入五级分类法（原子生成、条件生成、上下文生成、智能体生成、世界建模生成）来系统性地审视该领域的技术进展与评估缺陷。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视觉生成模型在真实感、指令遵循和交互编辑方面取得了显著进展，但在空间推理、持久状态、长程一致性和因果理解方面仍存在不足。作者认为该领域应超越外观合成，迈向基于结构、动力学、领域知识和因果关系的智能视觉生成。

Method: 提出一个五级分类法（Atomic Generation, Conditional Generation, In-Context Generation, Agentic Generation, World-Modeling Generation），从被动渲染器逐步演进到交互式、智能体化、世界感知的生成器；分析了关键技术驱动因素（流匹配、理解-生成统一模型、视觉表示改进、后训练、奖励建模、数据策展、合成数据蒸馏、采样加速）；通过基准测试回顾、野外压力测试和专家约束案例研究进行综合评估。

Result: 当前评估往往过度强调感知质量，低估了结构、时间和因果层面的失败，导致对进展的高估；智能视觉生成系统需要在结构、动态、知识和因果四个维度上做出实质性改进。

Conclusion: 视觉生成领域需要从被动渲染迈向智能生成，以能力为中心的分类法和评估框架有助于理解、评估和推动下一代智能视觉生成系统的发展。

Original Abstract: Recent visual generation models have made major progress in photorealism, typography, instruction following, and interactive editing, yet they still struggle with spatial reasoning, persistent state, long-horizon consistency, and causal understanding. We argue that the field should move beyond appearance synthesis toward intelligent visual generation: plausible visuals grounded in structure, dynamics, domain knowledge, and causal relations. To frame this shift, we introduce a five-level taxonomy: Atomic Generation, Conditional Generation, In-Context Generation, Agentic Generation, and World-Modeling Generation, progressing from passive renderers to interactive, agentic, world-aware generators. We analyze key technical drivers, including flow matching, unified understanding-and-generation models, improved visual representations, post-training, reward modeling, data curation, synthetic data distillation, and sampling acceleration. We further show that current evaluations often overestimate progress by emphasizing perceptual quality while missing structural, temporal, and causal failures. By combining benchmark review, in-the-wild stress tests, and expert-constrained case studies, this roadmap offers a capability-centered lens for understanding, evaluating, and advancing the next generation of intelligent visual generation systems.

中文摘要翻译: 近期视觉生成模型在照片真实感、排版、指令遵循和交互编辑方面取得了重大进展，但在空间推理、持久状态、长程一致性和因果理解方面仍然存在困难。我们认为该领域应超越外观合成，迈向智能视觉生成：即基于结构、动力学、领域知识和因果关系的合理视觉内容。为框定这一转变，我们引入了一个五级分类法：原子生成、条件生成、上下文生成、智能体生成和世界建模生成，从被动的渲染器逐步演进到交互式、智能体化、世界感知的生成器。我们分析了关键的技术驱动因素，包括流匹配、统一理解与生成模型、改进的视觉表示、后训练、奖励建模、数据策展、合成数据蒸馏和采样加速。我们进一步表明，当前的评估往往通过强调感知质量而忽略了结构、时间和因果上的失败，从而高估了进展。通过结合基准测试回顾、野外压力测试和专家约束案例研究，本路线图提供了一个以能力为中心的视角，用于理解、评估和推进下一代智能视觉生成系统。

</details>


### [59] [Representation Fréchet Loss for Visual Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28190)
*Jiawei Yang,Zhengyang Geng,Xuan Ju,Yonglong Tian,Yue Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出FD-loss，通过在表示空间中解耦FD估计的种群大小和梯度计算的批次大小，成功将Fréchet距离用作训练目标。实验表明，FD-loss能提升生成器视觉质量，将多步生成器转化为强一步生成器，并发现FID可能误导视觉质量评估，从而提出多表示评估指标FDr$^k$。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: Fréchet距离（FD）长期以来被认为不适合作为训练目标，本文旨在证明FD实际上可以在表示空间中被有效优化，从而突破这一认知局限。

Method: 将FD估计所需的种群大小（如50k）与梯度计算所需的批次大小（如1024）解耦，使得FD可以在表示空间中作为可优化的损失函数（FD-loss）进行训练。

Result: 1) 使用FD-loss后训练基础生成器，在Inception特征空间下，一步生成器在ImageNet 256×256上达到0.72 FID；2) FD-loss可将多步生成器转化为强一步生成器，无需教师蒸馏、对抗训练或逐样本目标；3) 发现FID可能错误排序视觉质量，现代表示空间可能产生更好样本但Inception FID更差，由此提出FDr$^k$多表示评估指标。

Conclusion: Fréchet距离在表示空间中可以作为有效的训练目标，并鼓励在多种表示空间中进一步探索分布距离作为生成模型的训练目标和评估指标。

Original Abstract: We show that Fréchet Distance (FD), long considered impractical as a training objective, can in fact be effectively optimized in the representation space. Our idea is simple: decouple the population size for FD estimation (e.g., 50k) from the batch size for gradient computation (e.g., 1024). We term this approach FD-loss. Optimizing FD-loss reveals several surprising findings. First, post-training a base generator with FD-loss in different representation spaces consistently improves visual quality. Under the Inception feature space, a one-step generator achieves0.72 FID on ImageNet 256x256. Second, the same FD-loss repurposes multi-step generators into strong one-step generators without teacher distillation, adversarial training or per-sample targets. Third, FID can misrank visual quality: modern representations can yield better samples despite worse Inception FID. This motivates FDr$^k$, a multi-representation metric. We hope this work will encourage further exploration of distributional distances in diverse representation spaces as both training objectives and evaluation metrics for generative models.

中文摘要翻译: 我们证明，长期以来被认为不适合作为训练目标的Fréchet距离（FD），实际上可以在表示空间中被有效优化。我们的想法很简单：将FD估计所需的种群大小（如50k）与梯度计算所需的批次大小（如1024）解耦。我们将此方法称为FD-loss。优化FD-loss揭示了几个令人惊讶的发现。首先，在不同表示空间中使用FD-loss对基础生成器进行后训练，能够持续提升视觉质量。在Inception特征空间下，一个一步生成器在ImageNet 256×256上达到了0.72的FID。其次，同样的FD-loss可以将多步生成器转化为强大的一步生成器，且无需教师蒸馏、对抗训练或逐样本目标。第三，FID可能错误排序视觉质量：现代表示空间可以产生更好的样本，但Inception FID却更差。这促使我们提出了多表示评估指标FDr$^k$。我们希望这项工作能鼓励在多种表示空间中进一步探索分布距离，将其作为生成模型的训练目标和评估指标。

</details>


### [60] [Generalizable Sparse-View 3D Reconstruction from Unconstrained Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28193)
*Vinayak Gupta,Chih-Hao Lin,Shenlong Wang,Anand Bhattad,Jia-Bin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GenWildSplat 提出了一种无需逐场景优化的前馈式框架，能够从稀疏无位姿的互联网图像中实时重建高质量3D场景，并在光照变化和瞬态遮挡下表现出优异的泛化能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法依赖外观嵌入或动态掩码进行逐场景优化，在稀疏视角下表现不佳，且由于评估场景有限，泛化能力存疑。因此需要一种无需逐场景优化、能在真实世界多变光照和遮挡条件下工作的稀疏视图重建方法。

Method: GenWildSplat 采用前馈式架构，从无位姿的稀疏图像中预测深度、相机参数和规范空间中的3D高斯。外观适配器根据目标光照调节外观，语义分割处理瞬态物体。通过课程学习在合成和真实数据上训练，使模型适应多样的光照和遮挡模式。

Result: 在 PhotoTourism 和 MegaScenes 基准上的评估表明，GenWildSplat 在渲染质量上达到了前馈式方法的最新水平，且无需测试时优化即可实现实时推理。

Conclusion: GenWildSplat 证明了基于前馈框架和课程学习策略可以有效解决稀疏、无位姿图像在真实场景下的3D重建问题，兼顾了高质量渲染与实时性能，具有强泛化能力。

Original Abstract: Reconstructing 3D scenes from sparse, unposed images remains challenging under real-world conditions with varying illumination and transient occlusions. Existing methods rely on scene-specific optimization using appearance embeddings or dynamic masks, which requires extensive per-scene training and fails under sparse views. Moreover, evaluations on limited scenes raise questions about generalization. We present GenWildSplat, a feed-forward framework for sparse-view outdoor reconstruction that requires no per-scene optimization. Given unposed internet images, GenWildSplat predicts depth, camera parameters, and 3D Gaussians in a canonical space using learned geometric priors. An appearance adapter modulates appearance for target lighting conditions, while semantic segmentation handles transient objects. Through curriculum learning on synthetic and real data, GenWildSplat generalizes across diverse illumination and occlusion patterns. Evaluations on PhotoTourism and MegaScenes benchmark demonstrate state-of-the-art feed-forward rendering quality, achieving real-time inference without test-time optimization

中文摘要翻译: 从稀疏且无位姿的图像中重建3D场景，在光照变化和瞬态遮挡的真实世界条件下仍然具有挑战性。现有方法依赖使用外观嵌入或动态掩码进行逐场景优化，这需要大量的逐场景训练，且在稀疏视角下表现不佳。此外，在有限场景上的评估引发了关于泛化能力的质疑。我们提出 GenWildSplat，一种用于稀疏视图室外重建的前馈式框架，无需逐场景优化。给定无位姿的互联网图像，GenWildSplat 利用学习到的几何先验，在规范空间中预测深度、相机参数和3D高斯。外观适配器根据目标光照条件调节外观，而语义分割则处理瞬态物体。通过在合成数据和真实数据上的课程学习，GenWildSplat 能够泛化到多样的光照和遮挡模式。在 PhotoTourism 和 MegaScenes 基准上的评估表明，GenWildSplat 在前馈式渲染质量上达到了最先进水平，无需测试时优化即可实现实时推理。

</details>


### [61] [HERMES++: Toward a Unified Driving World Model for 3D Scene Understanding and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28196)
*Xin Zhou,Dingkang Liang,Xiwu Chen,Feiyang Tan,Dingyuan Zhang,Hengshuang Zhao,Xiang Bai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HERMES++是一个统一的驾驶世界模型，通过将3D场景理解与未来几何预测整合在同一框架中，弥合了语义解释与物理模拟之间的鸿沟，在点云预测和场景理解任务上均超越专业方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有驾驶世界模型主要关注未来场景生成，缺乏全面的3D场景理解；而大语言模型虽有强大的推理能力，但无法预测未来几何演化。这两类任务之间存在显著鸿沟，亟需统一框架来同时实现语义理解与物理模拟。

Method: (1) BEV表示将多视角空间信息整合为与LLM兼容的结构；(2) LLM增强的世界查询促进理解分支的知识迁移；(3) Current-to-Future链接桥接时间间隙，将几何演化条件建立在语义上下文中；(4) 联合几何优化策略整合显式几何约束与隐式潜在正则化，对齐内部表示与几何先验。

Result: 在多个基准测试上的大量评估验证了方法的有效性。HERMES++取得了强劲性能，在未来点云预测和3D场景理解任务上均超越了专业方法。

Conclusion: HERMES++通过统一框架成功弥合了语义理解与物理模拟之间的差距，验证了联合建模3D场景理解与未来几何预测的可行性与优越性。

Original Abstract: Driving world models serve as a pivotal technology for autonomous driving by simulating environmental dynamics. However, existing approaches predominantly focus on future scene generation, often overlooking comprehensive 3D scene understanding. Conversely, while Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate impressive reasoning capabilities, they lack the capacity to predict future geometric evolution, creating a significant disparity between semantic interpretation and physical simulation. To bridge this gap, we propose HERMES++, a unified driving world model that integrates 3D scene understanding and future geometry prediction within a single framework. Our approach addresses the distinct requirements of these tasks through synergistic designs. First, a BEV representation consolidates multi-view spatial information into a structure compatible with LLMs. Second, we introduce LLM-enhanced world queries to facilitate knowledge transfer from the understanding branch. Third, a Current-to-Future Link is designed to bridge the temporal gap, conditioning geometric evolution on semantic context. Finally, to enforce structural integrity, we employ a Joint Geometric Optimization strategy that integrates explicit geometric constraints with implicit latent regularization to align internal representations with geometry-aware priors. Extensive evaluations on multiple benchmarks validate the effectiveness of our method. HERMES++ achieves strong performance, outperforming specialist approaches in both future point cloud prediction and 3D scene understanding tasks. The model and code will be publicly released at https://github.com/H-EmbodVis/HERMESV2.

中文摘要翻译: 驾驶世界模型通过模拟环境动态，成为自动驾驶的关键技术。然而，现有方法主要关注未来场景生成，往往忽视了全面的3D场景理解。反之，尽管大语言模型展现出令人印象深刻的推理能力，但它们缺乏预测未来几何演化的能力，造成了语义解释与物理模拟之间的显著差距。为弥合这一鸿沟，我们提出了HERMES++，一个统一的驾驶世界模型，将3D场景理解与未来几何预测整合在单一框架中。我们的方法通过协同设计来应对这些任务的不同需求。首先，BEV表示将多视角空间信息整合为与大语言模型兼容的结构。其次，我们引入LLM增强的世界查询，以促进从理解分支的知识迁移。第三，设计了从当前到未来的链接来桥接时间间隙，将几何演化条件建立在语义上下文之上。最后，为强化结构完整性，我们采用联合几何优化策略，整合显式几何约束与隐式潜在正则化，使内部表示与几何感知先验对齐。在多个基准测试上的大量评估验证了我们方法的有效性。HERMES++取得了强劲性能，在未来点云预测和3D场景理解任务上均超越了专业方法。模型和代码将在 https://github.com/H-EmbodVis/HERMESV2 公开发布。

</details>


### [62] [Benchmarking Deep Learning Models for Object Detection on Edge Computing Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2409.16808)
*Daghash K. Alqahtani,Aamir Cheema,Adel N. Toosi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文评估了YOLOv8、EfficientDet Lite和SSD系列目标检测模型在Raspberry Pi 3/4/5（带/不带TPU）和Jetson Orin Nano等边缘设备上的性能，包括能耗、推理时间和mAP，揭示了精度、速度与能效之间的权衡关系。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前对各类目标检测模型在资源受限的边缘设备上的效率和性能缺乏深入理解，无法为实际部署提供有效指导。

Method: 在Raspberry Pi 3/4/5（带/不带TPU加速器）和Jetson Orin Nano等主流边缘设备上部署YOLOv8（Nano, Small, Medium）、EfficientDet Lite（Lite0, Lite1, Lite2）和SSD（SSD MobileNet V1, SSDLite MobileDet）模型，收集并分析能耗、推理时间和mAP等关键性能指标。

Result: 低mAP模型（如SSD MobileNet V1）更节能且推理更快；高mAP模型（如YOLOv8 Medium）通常能耗更高、推理更慢，但在使用TPU加速器时存在例外；Jetson Orin Nano是处理请求最快且最节能的设备，尽管其空闲能耗最高。

Conclusion: 在边缘设备上部署深度学习模型时需要平衡精度、速度和能效，本文结果为从业者和研究者选择模型和设备提供了有价值的指导。

Original Abstract: Modern applications, such as autonomous vehicles, require deploying deep learning algorithms on resource-constrained edge devices for real-time image and video processing. However, there is limited understanding of the efficiency and performance of various object detection models on these devices. In this paper, we evaluate state-of-the-art object detection models, including YOLOv8 (Nano, Small, Medium), EfficientDet Lite (Lite0, Lite1, Lite2), and SSD (SSD MobileNet V1, SSDLite MobileDet). We deployed these models on popular edge devices like the Raspberry Pi 3, 4, and 5 with/without TPU accelerators, and Jetson Orin Nano, collecting key performance metrics such as energy consumption, inference time, and Mean Average Precision (mAP). Our findings highlight that lower mAP models such as SSD MobileNet V1 are more energy-efficient and faster in inference, whereas higher mAP models like YOLOv8 Medium generally consume more energy and have slower inference, though with exceptions when accelerators like TPUs are used. Among the edge devices, Jetson Orin Nano stands out as the fastest and most energy-efficient option for request handling, despite having the highest idle energy consumption. These results emphasize the need to balance accuracy, speed, and energy efficiency when deploying deep learning models on edge devices, offering valuable guidance for practitioners and researchers selecting models and devices for their applications.

中文摘要翻译: 现代应用（如自动驾驶汽车）需要在资源受限的边缘设备上部署深度学习算法以实现实时图像和视频处理。然而，目前对各类目标检测模型在这些设备上的效率和性能了解有限。本文评估了最先进的目标检测模型，包括YOLOv8（Nano、Small、Medium）、EfficientDet Lite（Lite0、Lite1、Lite2）和SSD（SSD MobileNet V1、SSDLite MobileDet）。我们将这些模型部署在树莓派3、4、5（带/不带TPU加速器）和Jetson Orin Nano等主流边缘设备上，收集了能耗、推理时间和平均精度均值（mAP）等关键性能指标。实验结果表明，SSD MobileNet V1等低mAP模型在能效和推理速度方面更具优势，而YOLOv8 Medium等高mAP模型通常能耗更高且推理更慢，但在使用TPU等加速器时存在例外。在所有边缘设备中，Jetson Orin Nano尽管空闲能耗最高，但在处理请求方面最快且能效最优。这些结果强调了在边缘设备上部署深度学习模型时需要平衡精度、速度和能效，为从业者和研究人员在选择模型和设备时提供了有价值的指导。
